data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vauxhall%27s,_Ellesmere_Port_-_geograph.org.uk_-_218503.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vauxhall_Ellesmere_Port" title="Vauxhall Ellesmere Port">Vauxhall\'s plant</a> in Ellesmere Port exports 88% of its cars, although many of the components are imported, and has made over 5 million since 1962, also making the <a href="/wiki/Opel_Vectra" title="Opel Vectra">Vectra</a> from 1995-2008; it makes 686 a day (two a minute, 100,000 a year) and the latest model was designed by <a href="/wiki/Mark_Adams_(designer)" title="Mark Adams (designer)">Mark Adams</a> and Malcolm Ward. 3m Astras have been bought in the UK since 1979, and featured on the <a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_test_track" title="Top Gear test track">Top Gear test track</a> until 2015; the production is split with the <a href="/wiki/Opel_Manufacturing_Poland" title="Opel Manufacturing Poland">Opel Manufacturing Poland</a> site at <a href="/wiki/Gliwice" title="Gliwice">Gliwice</a> in southern Poland; the <a href="/wiki/Opel_Corsa" title="Opel Corsa">Corsa</a> is made at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Opel_Zaragoza&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Opel Zaragoza (page does not exist)">Opel Zaragoza</a> in north-east Spain, with 3-door versions at <a href="/wiki/Opel_Eisenach" title="Opel Eisenach">Opel Eisenach</a>; the <a href="/wiki/Opel_Insignia" title="Opel Insignia">Insignia</a> is made at <a href="/wiki/Opel_R%C3%BCsselsheim" class="mw-redirect" title="Opel R\xc3\xbcsselsheim">Opel R\xc3\xbcsselsheim</a></div></div></div>\n<p>Cheshire is linked with the <a href="/wiki/Salt_in_Cheshire" title="Salt in Cheshire">salt industry</a>. <a href="/wiki/AstraZeneca" title="AstraZeneca">AstraZeneca</a>, the fifth largest pharmaceutical company in the world, has a manufacturing site in the north-east of Macclesfield on <a href="/wiki/Hurdsfield" class="mw-redirect" title="Hurdsfield">Hurdsfield</a> Ind Est (former ICI Pharmaceuticals) off the A523, where it makes Zoladex (<a href="/wiki/Goserelin" title="Goserelin">goserelin</a>); it was formerly ICI until June 1993 when it became <a href="/wiki/Zeneca" title="Zeneca">Zeneca</a>. <a href="/wiki/Vauxhall_Motors" title="Vauxhall Motors">Vauxhall</a>, home of the <a href="/wiki/Vauxhall_Astra" title="Vauxhall Astra">Astra</a>, is on a <a href="/wiki/RAF_Hooton_Park" title="RAF Hooton Park">former airfield</a> next to the <a href="/wiki/M53_motorway" title="M53 motorway">M53</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Stanlow_Refinery" title="Stanlow Refinery">Essar Energy</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_Shell" title="Royal Dutch Shell">Shell</a>, partly in <a href="/wiki/Thornton-le-Moors" title="Thornton-le-Moors">Thornton-le-Moors</a>) are in <a href="/wiki/Ellesmere_Port" title="Ellesmere Port">Ellesmere Port</a>. <a href="/wiki/SGS_S.A." title="SGS S.A.">SGS</a> UK, the world\'s leading industrial inspection organisation, is based off junction 8 of the M53 at Rossmore Business Park off the B5463. <a href="/wiki/Innospec" title="Innospec">Innospec</a> (former Octel) is west of the refinery near junction 9 of the M53 (<a href="/wiki/A5032_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A5032 road">A5032</a>); Innospec also has a site at Widnes (former Aroma Fine Chemicals) which makes <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lilestralis&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lilestralis (page does not exist)">Lilestralis</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Vidrala&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Vidrala (page does not exist)">Encirc Glass</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Aventas_group" title="Aventas group">Aventas group</a>) make glass bottles to the east of the refinery at <a href="/wiki/Elton,_Cheshire" title="Elton, Cheshire">Elton</a>; the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Shell_Technology_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Shell Technology Centre (page does not exist)">Shell Technology Centre</a> on the southern side of the <a href="/wiki/Ellesmere_Port_to_Warrington_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Ellesmere Port to Warrington Line">railway</a>, off the A5117 and the M56 <a href="/wiki/Hapsford" title="Hapsford">Hapsford</a> Interchange on the east side of the refinery, closed in 2014; to the east is the large site of <a href="/wiki/Kemira_GrowHow" title="Kemira GrowHow">CF Fertilisers</a> UK (former <a href="/w/index.php?title=Shellstar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Shellstar (page does not exist)">Shellstar</a>) who make the Nitram brand of fertiliser.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Lex_Autolease" title="Lex Autolease">Lex Autolease</a>, the UK\'s largest vehicle leasing company is in the east of Chester, towards <a href="/wiki/Hoole" title="Hoole">Hoole</a>. <a href="/wiki/Ball_Corporation" title="Ball Corporation">Ball Packaging Europe</a> is based on the <a href="/wiki/A483_road" title="A483 road">A483</a> at Chester Business Park, near the A55 junction in <a href="/wiki/Eccleston,_Cheshire" title="Eccleston, Cheshire">Eccleston</a>, which has a main office of <a href="/wiki/Marks_%26_Spencer" title="Marks &amp; Spencer">M&amp;S</a>; east of M&amp;S, south of the A55 bypass is <a href="/wiki/Sira_(group_of_British_companies)" class="mw-redirect" title="Sira (group of British companies)">Sira</a>, which issues <a href="/wiki/ATEX_directive" title="ATEX directive">ATEX</a> product approvals. To the north at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dunkirk,_Cheshire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dunkirk, Cheshire (page does not exist)">Dunkirk</a> at the end of the M56 on the <a href="/wiki/A5117_road" title="A5117 road">A5117</a>, is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Max_Spielmann&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Max Spielmann (page does not exist)">Max Spielmann</a> (including the former Klick) in <a href="/wiki/Lea-by-Backford" title="Lea-by-Backford">Lea-by-Backford</a>; further north at <a href="/wiki/Capenhurst" title="Capenhurst">Capenhurst</a>, next to the <a href="/wiki/Wirral_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Wirral Line">railway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Urenco_Group" title="Urenco Group">Urenco Group</a> have a <a href="/wiki/Enriched_uranium" title="Enriched uranium">uranium enrichment</a> plant, partly in <a href="/wiki/Ledsham,_Cheshire" title="Ledsham, Cheshire">Ledsham</a>. <a href="/wiki/Sandbach" title="Sandbach">Sandbach</a> used to be home of <a href="/wiki/ERF_(lorry_manufacturer)" class="mw-redirect" title="ERF (lorry manufacturer)">ERF</a> and <a href="/wiki/Edwin_Foden,_Sons_%26_Co." title="Edwin Foden, Sons &amp; Co.">Fodens</a> trucks. <a href="/wiki/Tata_Chemicals_Europe" title="Tata Chemicals Europe">Tata Chemicals Europe</a> (former Brunner Mond) next to the <a href="/wiki/A530_road" title="A530 road">A530</a>, next to the <a href="/wiki/Mid-Cheshire_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Mid-Cheshire Line">railway</a>, is partly in <a href="/wiki/Lostock_Gralam" title="Lostock Gralam">Lostock Gralam</a> just west of <a href="/wiki/Northwich" title="Northwich">Northwich</a>; there is another main site at <a href="/wiki/Winnington" title="Winnington">Winnington</a> on the <a href="/wiki/A533_road" title="A533 road">A533</a> north-west of Northwich. <a href="/wiki/British_Salt" title="British Salt">British Salt</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Middlewich" title="Middlewich">Middlewich</a>; <a href="/wiki/Bisto" title="Bisto">Bisto</a> used to be made there by Centura Foods (RHM), but production moved to <a href="/wiki/Worksop" title="Worksop">Worksop</a> (Nottinghamshire) in 2008. <a href="/wiki/Henkel" title="Henkel">Henkel UK</a> (the consumer adhesive division, maker of <a href="/wiki/Pritt" title="Pritt">Pritt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sellotape" title="Sellotape">Sellotape</a>) is on the Winsford Ind Estate in the east of <a href="/wiki/Winsford" title="Winsford">Winsford</a>, home of the UK\'s <a href="/wiki/Salt_in_Cheshire" title="Salt in Cheshire">largest</a> <a href="/wiki/Salt_mine" class="mw-redirect" title="Salt mine">salt mine</a> at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Meadowbank,_Cheshire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Meadowbank, Cheshire (page does not exist)">Meadowbank</a> run by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Salt_Union&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Salt Union (page does not exist)">Salt Union</a>, who are owned by <a href="/wiki/Compass_Minerals" title="Compass Minerals">Compass Minerals</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Mornflake" title="Mornflake">Mornflake</a> is in Crewe on the B5071, <a href="/wiki/Focus_(DIY)" class="mw-redirect" title="Focus (DIY)">Focus</a> closed in July 2011, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Orion_Optics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Orion Optics (page does not exist)">Orion Optics</a> make telescopes. <a href="/wiki/Bentley" title="Bentley">Bentley Motors</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Volkswagen" title="Volkswagen">Volkswagen</a> since 1998) have their <a href="/wiki/Bentley_Crewe" title="Bentley Crewe">main plant</a> in the west of the town between the <a href="/wiki/A530_road" title="A530 road">A530</a> and A532, next to the railway to Chester. <a href="/wiki/Crewe_Works" title="Crewe Works">Crewe Works</a> built the <a href="/wiki/InterCity_125" title="InterCity 125">HST</a> (<a href="/wiki/British_Rail_Class_43_(HST)" title="British Rail Class 43 (HST)">Class 43</a>) power cars, and now carries out maintenance for <a href="/wiki/Bombardier_Transportation" title="Bombardier Transportation">Bombardier</a>. <a href="/wiki/Unipart" title="Unipart">Unipart</a> Rail is on the B5071 next to Crewe railway station. <a href="/wiki/Bargain_Booze" title="Bargain Booze">Bargain Booze</a> is at the A532/A5020 roundabout in the east of the town, and further along the A532 <a href="/wiki/Whitby_Morrison" title="Whitby Morrison">Whitby Morrison</a> are the world\'s leading manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Ice_cream_van" title="Ice cream van">ice cream vans</a>. Air Products have a main HQ off the <a href="/wiki/A534_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A534 road">A534</a> in central Crewe near the Virgin Trains training academy. <a href="/w/index.php?title=UK_Fuels&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="UK Fuels (page does not exist)">UK Fuels</a> (<a href="/wiki/Fuel_card" title="Fuel card">fuel cards</a>) are off the A532, north of Crewe train station.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Land_%26_Armaments" title="BAE Systems Land &amp; Armaments">BAE Systems Global Combat Systems</a> at <a href="/wiki/ROF_Radway_Green" title="ROF Radway Green">Radway Green</a>, <a href="/wiki/Barthomley" title="Barthomley">Barthomley</a> north of M6 junction 16, south of <a href="/wiki/Alsager" title="Alsager">Alsager</a> makes small arms ammunition, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Freshpack&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Freshpack (page does not exist)">Freshpack</a> make pies next to the A5011 towards the east of the town; <a href="/wiki/Twyford_Bathrooms" title="Twyford Bathrooms">Twyford Bathrooms</a> (owned since 2001 by the Finnish <a href="/wiki/Sanitec" title="Sanitec">Sanitec</a>) are off the B5077, but their enormous factory next to the <a href="/wiki/Crewe_to_Derby_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Crewe to Derby Line">railway</a> closed in early 2011, with production moving overseas. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Oliver_Valves&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Oliver Valves (page does not exist)">Oliver Valves</a> based off the B5085 in Shaw Heath, Knutsford, makes <a href="/wiki/Needle_valve" title="Needle valve">needle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Check_valve" title="Check valve">check</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gate_valve" title="Gate valve">gate</a>, <a href="/wiki/Relief_valve" title="Relief valve">relief</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ball_valve" title="Ball valve">ball valves</a> for the oil and gas industry. Amec is south of Knutsford at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Booths_Hall&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Booths Hall (page does not exist)">Booths Hall</a> off the <a href="/wiki/A537_road" title="A537 road">A537</a>, now the HQ of <a href="/wiki/Amec_Foster_Wheeler" title="Amec Foster Wheeler">Amec Foster Wheeler</a>; also in the town is <a href="/wiki/Edmundson_Electrical" title="Edmundson Electrical">Edmundson Electrical</a>. Between Knutsford and Wilmslow in <a href="/wiki/Mobberley" title="Mobberley">Mobberley</a> off the B5085, close to the southern approach of Manchester Airport, is a large site of Harman Technology (known worldwide as <a href="/wiki/Ilford_Photo" title="Ilford Photo">Ilford Photo</a>). <a href="/wiki/Four_Seasons_Health_Care" title="Four Seasons Health Care">Four Seasons Health Care</a> is in central Wilmslow; north of the town on the <a href="/wiki/A538_road" title="A538 road">A538</a> is a large \xc2\xa360m mass spectrometry research site of the <a href="/wiki/Waters_Corporation" title="Waters Corporation">Waters Corporation</a>, built in 2014 on a former research site of <a href="/wiki/Ciba-Geigy" class="mw-redirect" title="Ciba-Geigy">Ciba-Geigy</a> Pharmaceuticals (who formed Novartis in 1996), next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Bollin" title="River Bollin">River Bollin</a>. <a href="/wiki/Pets_at_Home" title="Pets at Home">Pets at Home</a> is next to the <a href="/wiki/Crewe_to_Manchester_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Crewe to Manchester Line">railway</a> at <a href="/wiki/Handforth" title="Handforth">Handforth</a> near <a href="/wiki/Wilmslow" title="Wilmslow">Wilmslow</a> and the Stockport boundary near <a href="/wiki/Handforth_Dean" title="Handforth Dean">Handforth Dean</a> (A34). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Boalloy_Industries&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Boalloy Industries (page does not exist)">Boalloy Industries</a> are on Radnor Park Ind Est in <a href="/wiki/West_Heath,_Cheshire" title="West Heath, Cheshire">West Heath</a> in west Congleton north of the A534/A34 junction, make <a href="/wiki/Semi-trailer" title="Semi-trailer">trailers</a>, and pioneered the <a href="/wiki/Tautliner" title="Tautliner">Tautliner</a> curtain-sided trailer design in the 1970s. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Reginox&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reginox (page does not exist)">Reginox</a> UK (kitchen sinks) are in the north of Congleton; Siemens Industry Automation &amp; Drive Technologies UK make <a href="/wiki/Adjustable-speed_drive" title="Adjustable-speed drive">variable-speed drives</a>, exporting 98% of production, on Eaton Bank Trading Est near the <a href="/wiki/River_Dane" title="River Dane">River Dane</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Airbags_International&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Airbags International (page does not exist)">Airbags International</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/Autoliv" title="Autoliv">Autoliv</a>) make airbags on Congleton Business Park in <a href="/wiki/Hulme_Walfield" title="Hulme Walfield">Hulme Walfield</a>, on the north edge of the town. <a href="/wiki/OK_Diner" title="OK Diner">OK Diner</a> is in Macclesfield (previously in Middlewich); <a href="/wiki/Tullis_Russell" title="Tullis Russell">Tullis Russell</a> at <a href="/wiki/Bollington" title="Bollington">Bollington</a> makes the paper for all <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain_commemorative_stamps_2010%E2%80%9319" title="Great Britain commemorative stamps 2010\xe2\x80\x9319">Royal Mail stamps</a>, and has done for many years.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg/200px-View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg/300px-View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg/400px-View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:View_from_Helsby_Hill_-_geograph.org.uk_-_250843.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ineos ChlorVinyls at Runcorn in 2006; the <a href="/wiki/Chemical_industry_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Chemical industry in the United Kingdom">UK chemicals industry</a> is worth \xc2\xa357bn, with 180,000 people in around 3,000 companies</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Ineos" title="Ineos">Ineos</a> Fluor (the site was previously owned by <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Chemical_Industries" title="Imperial Chemical Industries">ICI Chemicals</a>) is at Runcorn which produces chlorine and caustic soda from Cheshire salt, piped from <a href="/wiki/Lostock_Gralam" title="Lostock Gralam">Lostock Gralam</a>, south of Northwich; most of the chlorine in the UK comes from this plant; it also makes <a href="/wiki/Organofluorine_chemistry" title="Organofluorine chemistry">hydrofluoroalkanes</a> (HFAs) for <a href="/wiki/Metered-dose_inhaler" title="Metered-dose inhaler">metered-dose inhalers</a> and the anaesthetic <a href="/wiki/Halothane" title="Halothane">halothane</a>. There is Ineos Chlor and Ineos Vinyls. <a href="/wiki/BNFL" class="mw-redirect" title="BNFL">BNFL</a> and its subsidiary <a href="/wiki/Sellafield_Ltd" title="Sellafield Ltd">Sellafield Ltd</a> (former British Nuclear Group), and <a href="/wiki/ABB_Group" title="ABB Group">ABB UK</a> are based in <a href="/wiki/Daresbury" title="Daresbury">Daresbury</a> near Runcorn, although most of BNG\'s operations take place at <a href="/wiki/Sellafield" title="Sellafield">Sellafield</a> in Cumbria. Daresbury is also home of the <a href="/wiki/EMMA_(accelerator)" title="EMMA (accelerator)">EMMA</a> and <a href="/wiki/ALICE_(accelerator)" title="ALICE (accelerator)">ALICE</a> <a href="/wiki/FFAG_accelerator" title="FFAG accelerator">FFAG accelerators</a>. <a href="/wiki/Diageo" title="Diageo">Diageo</a> bottles <a href="/wiki/Guinness" title="Guinness">Guinness</a> at <a href="/wiki/Preston_Brook" title="Preston Brook">Preston Brook</a>, between the A56 and <a href="/wiki/A533_road" title="A533 road">A533</a>, and nearby <a href="/wiki/Saint-Gobain" title="Saint-Gobain">Saint-Gobain</a> UK make Isover insulation. <a href="/wiki/Kawneer" title="Kawneer">Kawneer</a> UK (part of <a href="/wiki/Alcoa" title="Alcoa">Alcoa</a>) make architectural aluminium systems (<a href="/wiki/Curtain_wall_(architecture)" title="Curtain wall (architecture)">curtain walls</a>) off the <a href="/wiki/A533_road" title="A533 road">A533</a> at <a href="/wiki/Astmoor" title="Astmoor">Astmoor</a> in north Runcorn. <a href="/wiki/APPH" title="APPH">APPH</a> (aircraft <a href="/wiki/Landing_gear" title="Landing gear">undercarriage</a>) is based off the A558 on <a href="/w/index.php?title=Manor_Park_(Runcorn)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Manor Park (Runcorn) (page does not exist)">Manor Park</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sandymoor" title="Sandymoor">Sandymoor</a> near <a href="/w/index.php?title=TALL_Security_Print&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="TALL Security Print (page does not exist)">TALL Security Print</a>, the UK\'s leading provider of business cheques; further to the west is <a href="/wiki/Yokogawa_Electric" title="Yokogawa Electric">Yokogawa Electric</a> UK. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Schachihata&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Schachihata (page does not exist)">Schachihata</a> UK (<a href="/w/index.php?title=Xstamper&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Xstamper (page does not exist)">Xstamper</a> and <a href="/wiki/Artline_(marker)" class="mw-redirect" title="Artline (marker)">Artline</a>) are based at Ashville Ind Est on the <a href="/wiki/A557_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A557 road">A557</a> at junction 12 of the M56 next to the Weaver Navigation and the 3,200&#160;ft <a href="/wiki/Weaver_Viaduct" title="Weaver Viaduct">Weaver Viaduct</a> south of Runcorn towards <a href="/wiki/Sutton_Weaver" title="Sutton Weaver">Sutton Weaver</a>. At the A5080 junction in Widnes, on the western side of the A557 is a <a href="/w/index.php?title=Marley_Eternit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Marley Eternit (page does not exist)">Marley Eternit</a> plant (<a href="/wiki/Eternit" title="Eternit">Eternit</a> roofing), and on the other side is a plant of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Rockwood_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rockwood (company) (page does not exist)">Rockwood Additives</a> UK (former <a href="/wiki/Laporte_plc" title="Laporte plc">Laporte</a>). <a href="/wiki/Croda_International" title="Croda International">Croda</a> Enterprise Technology Group does its important R&amp;D in <a href="/wiki/Halebank" title="Halebank">Halebank</a>, Widnes, south of <a href="/wiki/Ditton,_Cheshire" title="Ditton, Cheshire">Ditton</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Thermphos_International" title="Thermphos International">Thermphos</a> factory on the A557 south of Widnes closed in 2013.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/United_Utilities" title="United Utilities">United Utilities</a> is based in the west of Warrington at Lingley Mere Business Park in <a href="/wiki/Great_Sankey" title="Great Sankey">Great Sankey</a>, next to the St Helens boundary; in Lingley Green to the south on the A57 was the former HQ of <a href="/wiki/North_West_Water" title="North West Water">North West Water</a>; to the north, Amazon have a fulfilment centre. Unilever makes <i><a href="/wiki/Persil" title="Persil">Persil</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Surf_(detergent)" title="Surf (detergent)">Surf</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Laundry_detergent" title="Laundry detergent">washing powders</a> next to the <a href="/wiki/Warrington_Bank_Quay_railway_station" title="Warrington Bank Quay railway station">Bank Quay</a> railway station; next door between the <a href="/wiki/A5061_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A5061 road">A5061</a> and River Mersey is <a href="/w/index.php?title=PQ_Corporation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="PQ Corporation (page does not exist)">PQ Silicas</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Crosfield" title="Joseph Crosfield">Joseph Crosfield</a>). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cogent_Skills&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cogent Skills (page does not exist)">Cogent Skills</a> (the UK\'s <a href="/wiki/Sector_Skills_Councils" title="Sector Skills Councils">SSC</a> for science) is in the south of Warrington off the A5060, on the other side of the <a href="/wiki/Ellesmere_Port_to_Warrington_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Ellesmere Port to Warrington Line">railway</a> from Bank Quay. <a href="/wiki/New_Balance" title="New Balance">New Balance</a> UK is at Centre Park, off the A5060 in south-west Warrington, with a factory at <a href="/wiki/Flimby" title="Flimby">Flimby</a>, on the Cumbria coast. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Konftel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Konftel (page does not exist)">Konftel UK</a> is at <a href="/wiki/Thelwall" title="Thelwall">Thelwall</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Eagle_Ottawa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Eagle Ottawa (page does not exist)">Eagle Ottawa</a> makes leather upholstery for cars off the <a href="/wiki/A50_road" title="A50 road">A50</a> at Westy Park in east Warrington next to the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_Ship_Canal" title="Manchester Ship Canal">Manchester Ship Canal</a>. <a href="/wiki/ASICS" title="ASICS">ASICS</a> UK (sportswear) is on the Gemini Business Park, off the A574 in <a href="/wiki/Burtonwood_and_Westbrook" class="mw-redirect" title="Burtonwood and Westbrook">Burtonwood and Westbrook</a> north of Warrington, next to the M62 and a large IKEA and M&amp;S on Gemini Retail Park; next door is <a href="/wiki/KYB" class="mw-redirect" title="KYB">KYB</a> UK, part of the world\'s largest (Japanese) manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Shock_absorber" title="Shock absorber">shock absorbers</a>; nearby is <a href="/wiki/Krauss-Maffei" title="Krauss-Maffei">Krauss-Maffei</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Injection_molding_machine" title="Injection molding machine">injection moulding machines</a>); AlphaBiolabs provide the <a href="/wiki/DNA_paternity_testing" title="DNA paternity testing">DNA paternity testing</a> for <i><a href="/wiki/The_Jeremy_Kyle_Show" title="The Jeremy Kyle Show">The Jeremy Kyle Show</a></i> on Carina Park in <a href="/wiki/Westbrook,_Cheshire" title="Westbrook, Cheshire">Westbrook</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Burtonwood_Brewery&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Burtonwood Brewery (page does not exist)">Burtonwood Brewery</a> (the HQ of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Thomas_Hardy_Burtonwood&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Thomas Hardy Burtonwood (page does not exist)">Thomas Hardy Burtonwood</a>, who developed Britain\'s <a href="/wiki/Alcopop" title="Alcopop">alcopop</a> drinks in the 1990s) is on the B5204 in the west of Burtonwood, towards St Helens borough. Birchwood Park has to be the main technical business park in the North West. The Bank of England <a href="/wiki/Monetary_Policy_Committee" title="Monetary Policy Committee">MPC</a>\'s Agency for the North West is on <a href="/wiki/Birchwood_Park" title="Birchwood Park">Birchwood Park</a> near the HQ of <a href="/w/index.php?title=GB_Oils&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="GB Oils (page does not exist)">GB Oils</a>, the UK\'s leading fuel oil supplier (owned by <a href="/wiki/DCC_Plc" class="mw-redirect" title="DCC Plc">DCC</a>), and the operator of <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Oil_UK" class="mw-redirect" title="Gulf Oil UK">Gulf Oil</a> petrol stations in the UK. <a href="/wiki/Electricity_North_West" title="Electricity North West">Electricity North West</a> (the North West\'s <a href="/wiki/Distribution_network_operator" title="Distribution network operator">distribution network operator</a>) is near by, with <a href="/wiki/ESR_Technology" title="ESR Technology">ESR Technology</a>, who did work for the <a href="/wiki/Philae_(spacecraft)" title="Philae (spacecraft)">Philae</a> space probe and owns the <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Centre_of_Tribology&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="National Centre of Tribology (page does not exist)">National Centre of Tribology</a> at Whittle House in Risley, with <a href="/wiki/TalkTalk_Business" title="TalkTalk Business">TalkTalk Business</a> to the west, near <a href="/wiki/International_Nuclear_Services" title="International Nuclear Services">International Nuclear Services</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sellafield_Ltd" title="Sellafield Ltd">Sellafield Ltd</a> at <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Hinton,_Baron_Hinton_of_Bankside" title="Christopher Hinton, Baron Hinton of Bankside">Hinton House</a>. <a href="/wiki/Terberg_Group" title="Terberg Group">Terberg</a> Matec UK (Dutch) supply lifts for bin wagons next to M62 junction 11. Also west of the park is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Nuvia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nuvia (page does not exist)">Nuvia</a> UK (part of <a href="/wiki/Soletanche_Freyssinet" class="mw-redirect" title="Soletanche Freyssinet">Soletanche Freyssinet</a>). <a href="/wiki/Betfred" title="Betfred">Betfred</a> (having the largest turnover in the region\xe2\x80\x94\xc2\xa313.3bn) is at the western end of Birchwood itself, next to the M6 and <a href="/wiki/Birchwood_railway_station" title="Birchwood railway station">Birchwood railway station</a>. Birchwood was built on the former <a href="/wiki/ROF_Risley" title="ROF Risley">ROF Risley</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lancashire_2">Lancashire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Lancashire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Lancashire#Economy" title="Lancashire">Lancashire \xc2\xa7&#160;Economy</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Canberra,_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Canberra%2C_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg/220px-Canberra%2C_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Canberra%2C_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg/330px-Canberra%2C_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Canberra%2C_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg/440px-Canberra%2C_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="427" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Canberra,_Samlesbury_-_geograph.org.uk_-_101508.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/English_Electric_Canberra" title="English Electric Canberra">English Electric Canberra</a> <a href="/wiki/Gate_guardian" title="Gate guardian">gate guard</a> at <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Military_Air_%26_Information" title="BAE Systems Military Air &amp; Information">BAE\'s</a> <a href="/wiki/Samlesbury_Aerodrome" title="Samlesbury Aerodrome">Samlesbury</a> site</div></div></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Office_for_National_Statistics" title="Office for National Statistics">ONS</a> 2010 Annual Business Survey states that 30.3% of jobs in the British aerospace industry are based in Lancashire.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> The main private employer in the county is <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Military_Air_%26_Information" title="BAE Systems Military Air &amp; Information">BAE Systems Military Air &amp; Information</a> who have two sites east and west of <a href="/wiki/Preston,_Lancashire" title="Preston, Lancashire">Preston</a> for the manufacture of military aircraft. <a href="/wiki/Samlesbury_Aerodrome" title="Samlesbury Aerodrome">Samlesbury</a> (4000 employees) makes air-frames; the front fuselage, canards and tailfin of the Eurofighter. <a href="/wiki/Warton_Aerodrome" title="Warton Aerodrome">Warton</a>, BAE Systems\' main site (former <a href="/wiki/English_Electric" title="English Electric">English Electric</a>, then <a href="/wiki/British_Aircraft_Corporation" title="British Aircraft Corporation">BAC</a>), in <a href="/wiki/Bryning-with-Warton" title="Bryning-with-Warton">Bryning-with-Warton</a> (6500 employees).<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> BAE builds a Eurofighter every two weeks (<a href="/wiki/Takt_time" title="Takt time">takt time</a>). <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_plc" class="mw-redirect" title="Rolls-Royce plc">Rolls-Royce</a> make <a href="/wiki/Turbofan" title="Turbofan">turbofan</a> blades in <a href="/wiki/Barnoldswick" title="Barnoldswick">Barnoldswick</a> (950 employees).<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Nearby Weston EU manufacture components in <a href="/wiki/Foulridge" title="Foulridge">Foulridge</a> (250)<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> and engine maintenance contractor <a href="/w/index.php?title=Euravia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Euravia (page does not exist)">Euravia</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Kelbrook" title="Kelbrook">Kelbrook</a> (100).<sup id="cite_ref-LTRecr_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTRecr-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Safran" title="Safran">Safran</a> Aircelle make engine <a href="/wiki/Nacelle" title="Nacelle">nacelles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thrust_reversal" title="Thrust reversal">thrust reversers</a> in <a href="/wiki/Burnley" title="Burnley">Burnley</a> (800), and mostly make thrust reversers for the <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Trent_700" title="Rolls-Royce Trent 700">Trent 700</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/GE" class="mw-redirect" title="GE">GE</a> subsidiary Unison Engine Components (320),<sup id="cite_ref-LTRecr_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTRecr-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> are the largest of several others in the area.\n</p><p>(<a href="/wiki/Westinghouse_Electric_Company" title="Westinghouse Electric Company">Westinghouse</a>) (BNFL) make <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_fuel" title="Nuclear fuel">nuclear fuel</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Springfields" title="Springfields">Springfields</a> site at <a href="/wiki/Salwick" title="Salwick">Salwick</a>, off the <a href="/wiki/A583_road" title="A583 road">A583</a> in <a href="/wiki/Newton_with_Clifton" title="Newton with Clifton">Newton with Clifton</a>. The boiler firm <a href="/wiki/BAXI" class="mw-redirect" title="BAXI">BAXI</a> have a factory in the south of Preston, and next door, <a href="/wiki/Assystem" title="Assystem">Assystem</a> UK (engineering consultancy) are off the B5258 in <a href="/wiki/Bamber_Bridge" title="Bamber Bridge">Bamber Bridge</a>. <a href="/wiki/Anheuser-Busch_InBev" title="Anheuser-Busch InBev">AB InBev</a> have a brewery on the B6230 in nearby in <a href="/wiki/Samlesbury" title="Samlesbury">Samlesbury</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Whitbread" title="Whitbread">Whitbread</a>, and brews <a href="/wiki/Stella_Artois" title="Stella Artois">Stella Artois</a>); further east the BAE Systems factory is between the A677 and A59, mainly in <a href="/wiki/Balderstone,_Lancashire" title="Balderstone, Lancashire">Balderstone</a>. To the north-east of Preston, Bodycare Group make toiletries at the Red Scar Business Park on the B6243, near junction 31a of the M6, where <a href="/w/index.php?title=Goss_International&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Goss International (page does not exist)">Goss International</a> UK make <a href="/wiki/Printing_press" title="Printing press">printing presses</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Webb_Ivory&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Webb Ivory (page does not exist)">Webb Ivory</a> (charity fundraising, owned by <a href="/wiki/Findel_plc" title="Findel plc">Findel plc</a>) is off the A6 in <a href="/wiki/Avenham" title="Avenham">Avenham</a>, in the south of Preston. <a href="/wiki/Alstom" title="Alstom">Alstom</a> Transport (former <a href="/wiki/GEC_Traction" title="GEC Traction">GEC Traction</a>) is at TLS Preston; company\'s main Trafford Park site closed in the early 1990s. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Bosal_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bosal (company) (page does not exist)">Bosal</a> was the UK\'s leading manufacturer of car exhausts on Walton Summit, between the M6 and M61 until they closed operations. The Pilkington European Technical Centre is at <a href="/wiki/Lathom" title="Lathom">Lathom</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Oaktec&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Oaktec (page does not exist)">Oaktec</a> are small motorsport company on the <a href="/wiki/A588_road" title="A588 road">A588</a> at <a href="/wiki/Cockerham" title="Cockerham">Cockerham</a>, south of Lancaster. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Standfast_%26_Barracks&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Standfast &amp; Barracks (page does not exist)">Standfast &amp; Barracks</a> make high-end intricately designed furnishings on the A683 north of Lancaster, next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Lune" title="River Lune">River Lune</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Voith" title="Voith">Voith</a> Paper have a site in <a href="/wiki/Stubbins" title="Stubbins">Stubbins</a>, at the northern end of the M66, off the <a href="/wiki/A676_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A676 road">A676</a>. <a href="/wiki/Silentnight" title="Silentnight">Silentnight</a> (600)<sup id="cite_ref-LTRecr_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTRecr-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> is in <a href="/wiki/Barnoldswick" title="Barnoldswick">Barnoldswick</a>, where <a href="/wiki/Hope_Technology" title="Hope Technology">Hope Technology</a> make mountain bike components; nearby <a href="/wiki/Johnson_Matthey" title="Johnson Matthey">Johnson Matthey</a> make automotive catalysts. At <a href="/wiki/Whitworth,_Lancashire" title="Whitworth, Lancashire">Whitworth</a> on the A671, BCH engineer equipment for the food processing industry (<a href="/wiki/Nestl%C3%A9" title="Nestl\xc3\xa9">Nestl\xc3\xa9</a> and Mars).\n</p><p>Brands originating in Lancashire include: <a href="/wiki/TVR" title="TVR">TVR</a>, <a href="/wiki/Reebok" title="Reebok">Reebok</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Cars" title="Jaguar Cars">Jaguar Cars</a> and <a href="/wiki/Warburtons" title="Warburtons">Warburtons</a>. <a href="/wiki/Leyland_Trucks" title="Leyland Trucks">Leyland Trucks</a> manufactures several truck ranges from <a href="/wiki/Leyland,_Lancashire" title="Leyland, Lancashire">Leyland</a>, home of <a href="/wiki/Enterprise_plc" title="Enterprise plc">Enterprise plc</a>, and where <a href="/wiki/Albion_Motors" title="Albion Motors">Albion Automotive</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/American_Axle" title="American Axle">American Axle</a>) make <a href="/wiki/Crankshaft" title="Crankshaft">crankshafts</a> at <a href="/wiki/Farington" title="Farington">Farington</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=CCA_Occasions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="CCA Occasions (page does not exist)">CCA Occasions</a> makes greeting cards on the B5253 on the <a href="/wiki/Moss_Side,_South_Ribble" title="Moss Side, South Ribble">Moss Side</a> Ind Estate and nearby <a href="/wiki/Dr_Oetker" class="mw-redirect" title="Dr Oetker">Dr Oetker</a> makes Chicago Town and Pizza Ristorante pizzas (330);<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> 40% of the UK\'s frozen pizzas are made here, and the Pizza Ristorante brand, solely made in Lancashire, is Italy\'s best-selling frozen pizza with 20% of the Italian market.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Nearby, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Nitecrest&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nitecrest (page does not exist)">Nitecrest</a> is the UK\'s leading manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Gift_card" title="Gift card">gift</a>, <a href="/wiki/Payment_card" title="Payment card">payment</a>, <a href="/wiki/Loyalty_program" title="Loyalty program">loyalty</a> and <a href="/wiki/Telephone_card" title="Telephone card">phone cards</a>, and exports most of its products.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Walkers_(snack_foods)" title="Walkers (snack foods)">Walker\'s</a> make <a href="/wiki/Monster_Munch" title="Monster Munch">Monster Munch</a> at junction 5 of the M58 on the Pimbo Ind Est in <a href="/wiki/Upholland" title="Upholland">Up Holland</a>; nearby <a href="/wiki/Svenska_Cellulosa_Aktiebolaget" class="mw-redirect" title="Svenska Cellulosa Aktiebolaget">SCA Hygiene</a> has their Skelmersdale Mill which makes <a href="/wiki/Paper_towel" title="Paper towel">kitchen towel</a>, with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Uretek&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Uretek (page does not exist)">Uretek</a> UK (polyurethane). To the east is <a href="/wiki/Frederick%27s_Dairies" title="Frederick&#39;s Dairies">Frederick\'s Dairies</a> in East Pimbo, who make Cadbury\'s ice creams, near <a href="/w/index.php?title=TAAG_Steelwork&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="TAAG Steelwork (page does not exist)">TAAG Steelwork</a>, who built the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Olympic_Energy_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Olympic Energy Centre (page does not exist)">Olympic Energy Centre</a>. To the west, <a href="/wiki/Turtle_Wax" title="Turtle Wax">Turtle Wax</a> Europe are next to M58 junction 4 on Gillibrands Ind Est. <a href="/wiki/The_Co-operative_Bank" title="The Co-operative Bank">The Co-operative Bank</a> are administered from Delf House in the centre of Skelmersdale.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Victrex" title="Victrex">Victrex</a> make <a href="/wiki/PEEK" class="mw-redirect" title="PEEK">PEEK</a> (a <a href="/wiki/Thermoplastic" title="Thermoplastic">thermoplastic</a>) just north of Blackpool at <a href="/wiki/Cleveleys" title="Cleveleys">Cleveleys</a>. Next door, AGC Chemicals Europe, owned by <a href="/wiki/Asahi_Glass_Co." class="mw-redirect" title="Asahi Glass Co.">Asahi Glass Co.</a>, makes <a href="/wiki/ETFE" title="ETFE">ETFE</a> (fluon) for <a href="/wiki/Electrical_wiring" title="Electrical wiring">electrical wire insulation</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Silica_gel" title="Silica gel">silica gel</a> off the B5268 at <a href="/wiki/Thornton-Cleveleys" title="Thornton-Cleveleys">Thornton-Cleveleys</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=HTI_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HTI Group (page does not exist)">HTI Group</a> in Fleetwood makes toys and owns <a href="/wiki/Barbie" title="Barbie">Barbie</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ennis_Prismo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ennis Prismo (page does not exist)">Ennis Prismo</a> make traffic white line products at Chorley; Walmsleys is a paper manufacturer off the A675 in <a href="/wiki/Withnell" title="Withnell">Withnell</a>. <a href="/wiki/DXC_Technology" title="DXC Technology">DXC Technology</a> (former CSC) have sites in Chorley and Preston. Along the M65, Fort Vale based in <a href="/wiki/Simonstone,_Lancashire" title="Simonstone, Lancashire">Simonstone</a> (near <a href="/wiki/Burnley" title="Burnley">Burnley</a>) (300) are a world leader in valves and fittings for <a href="/wiki/Tank_truck" title="Tank truck">road tankers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Close by, office furniture manufacturer Senator International (800)<sup id="cite_ref-LTRecr_49-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTRecr-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> and household plastic container manufacturer What More UK (170)<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> are the largest in the UK in their respective fields. Off the A646 in <a href="/wiki/Habergham_Eaves" title="Habergham Eaves">Habergham Eaves</a>, east of Burnley, is <a href="/wiki/AMS_Neve" title="AMS Neve">AMS Neve</a>, a renowned manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Mixing_console" title="Mixing console">audio mixing desks</a>. Telecoms provider <a href="/wiki/Daisy_Group" title="Daisy Group">Daisy Group</a> (former Pipex,400),<sup id="cite_ref-LTRecr_49-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTRecr-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> based in <a href="/wiki/Nelson,_Lancashire" title="Nelson, Lancashire">Nelson</a> is one of the UK\'s fastest growing companies, on Lomeshaye Ind Est north of M65 junction 12 in <a href="/wiki/Brierfield,_Lancashire" title="Brierfield, Lancashire">Brierfield</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Cott" title="Cott">Cott Beverages</a> (former <a href="/w/index.php?title=Macaw_Soft_Drinks&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Macaw Soft Drinks (page does not exist)">Macaw Soft Drinks</a> before 2006) is off junction 12 of the M65 in <a href="/wiki/Brierfield,_Lancashire" title="Brierfield, Lancashire">Brierfield</a>, west of Nelson, next to <a href="/wiki/Pendle_Water" title="Pendle Water">Pendle Water</a>. <a href="/wiki/Jura_Elektroapparate" title="Jura Elektroapparate">Jura</a> UK (Swiss coffee machines) is off the A6068 in Colne. At <a href="/w/index.php?title=Horrocksford&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Horrocksford (page does not exist)">Horrocksford</a> near Clitheroe, <a href="/wiki/Hanson_Cement" title="Hanson Cement">Hanson Cement</a> have their large <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ribblesdale_Cement&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ribblesdale Cement (page does not exist)">Ribblesdale Cement</a> works, next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Ribble" title="River Ribble">River Ribble</a>, which supplied construction of the <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Metropolitan_Cathedral" title="Liverpool Metropolitan Cathedral">Liverpool Metropolitan Cathedral</a>. <a href="/wiki/Bensons_for_Beds" title="Bensons for Beds">Bensons for Beds</a> (previously in <a href="/wiki/Burtonwood_and_Westbrook" class="mw-redirect" title="Burtonwood and Westbrook">Burtonwood</a> near Warrington) and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Sleepmasters&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sleepmasters (page does not exist)">Sleepmasters</a> (both owned by <a href="/wiki/Steinhoff_International" title="Steinhoff International">Steinhoff International</a>) are in the north of Accrington, off junction 8 (A56) of the M65, near <a href="/wiki/Huncoat_railway_station" title="Huncoat railway station">Huncoat railway station</a>. <a href="/wiki/Kleeneze" title="Kleeneze">Kleeneze</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Findel_plc" title="Findel plc">Findel plc</a>) is based with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Express_Gifts&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Express Gifts (page does not exist)">Express Gifts</a> off the <a href="/wiki/A678_road" title="A678 road">A678</a> in <a href="/wiki/Clayton-le-Moors" title="Clayton-le-Moors">Clayton-le-Moors</a> off the M65 Hyndburn Interchange between Blackburn and Burnley, north of Accrington with a main distribution centre off the A679 in <a href="/wiki/Church,_Lancashire" title="Church, Lancashire">Church</a> on the other side of the M65 in the west of Accrington, with both sites next to the Leeds-Liverpool Canal. Off the <a href="/wiki/A678_road" title="A678 road">A678</a> near the River Calder in <a href="/wiki/Altham,_Lancashire" title="Altham, Lancashire">Altham</a> (north east of Clayton le Moors) is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Senator_(furniture)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Senator (furniture) (page does not exist)">Senator</a> who claim to be the UK\'s largest manufacturer of office furniture; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Simon_Jersey&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Simon Jersey (page does not exist)">Simon Jersey</a> designed and made the <a href="/wiki/Team_GB" title="Team GB">Team GB</a> clothing for the <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics" title="Great Britain at the 2016 Summer Olympics">2016 Olympics</a> opening and closing ceremonies.\n</p><p>In Blackpool is the <a href="/wiki/Federation_of_Small_Businesses" title="Federation of Small Businesses">Federation of Small Businesses</a> (FSB), <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amber_Taverns&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Amber Taverns (page does not exist)">Amber Taverns</a>, <a href="/wiki/Premium_Bond" title="Premium Bond">Premium Bonds</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Savings_and_Investments" title="National Savings and Investments">National Savings and Investments</a>. <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Eagle" title="Dennis Eagle">Dennis Eagle</a> makes bin wagons in Marton; <a href="/wiki/Tangerine_Confectionery" title="Tangerine Confectionery">Tangerine Confectionery</a> are based at Little Marton, with another factory to the east, just south of the main government building site. The <a href="/wiki/Service_Personnel_and_Veterans_Agency" title="Service Personnel and Veterans Agency">Service Personnel and Veterans Agency</a> (MoD\'s pensions, former <a href="/wiki/Veterans_Agency" title="Veterans Agency">Veterans Agency</a>) is off the <a href="/wiki/A585_road" title="A585 road">A585</a> in east Blackpool at the B268 roundabout at Norcross in the south of <a href="/wiki/Anchorsholme" title="Anchorsholme">Anchorsholme</a>. The NS &amp; I office of Blackpool is on the <a href="/wiki/A583_road" title="A583 road">A583</a>, off the M55 Marton Circle, in <a href="/wiki/Marton,_Blackpool" title="Marton, Blackpool">Little Marton</a> on the eastern edge of the town. <a href="/wiki/Disability_Living_Allowance" title="Disability Living Allowance">Disability Living Allowance</a>, replaced by <a href="/wiki/Personal_Independence_Payment" title="Personal Independence Payment">Personal Independence Payment</a>, is administered by the DWP, with the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Disablement_Services_Authority&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Disablement Services Authority (page does not exist)">Disablement Services Authority</a> at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Warbreck_House&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Warbreck House (page does not exist)">Warbreck House</a> west of the <a href="/wiki/A587_road" title="A587 road">A587</a>, accessed from the B5265 and next to <a href="/wiki/Bispham_High_School_Arts_College" title="Bispham High School Arts College">Bispham High School</a>. At the end of the M55 (junction 4) off the A5230 in <a href="/wiki/Westby-with-Plumptons" title="Westby-with-Plumptons">Westby-with-Plumptons</a> is DWP\'s large <a href="/w/index.php?title=Peel_Park_Control_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Peel Park Control Centre (page does not exist)">Peel Park Control Centre</a>, on the Blackpool boundary. Amber Taverns is near <a href="/wiki/Blackpool_North_railway_station" title="Blackpool North railway station">Blackpool North railway station</a>. To the north of Peel Park, next to the Clifton Retail Park in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mereside&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mereside (page does not exist)">Mereside</a> is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Glasdon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Glasdon (page does not exist)">Glasdon</a> (<a href="/wiki/Street_furniture" title="Street furniture">roadside furniture</a>), off the A583.\n<a href="/wiki/Burton%27s_Biscuit_Company" title="Burton&#39;s Biscuit Company">Burton\'s Biscuit Company</a> (owned since November 2013 by the <a href="/wiki/Ontario_Teachers%27_Pension_Plan" title="Ontario Teachers&#39; Pension Plan">Ontario Teachers\' Pension Plan</a>) have many head office functions in <a href="/wiki/Layton,_Blackpool" title="Layton, Blackpool">Layton, Blackpool</a> and a factory off the B5124, in the south of Warbreck, next to the <a href="/wiki/Blackpool_Branch_Lines" class="mw-redirect" title="Blackpool Branch Lines">railway line</a>, which makes <a href="/wiki/Maryland_Cookies" title="Maryland Cookies">Maryland Cookies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cadbury_Fingers" title="Cadbury Fingers">Cadbury Fingers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wagon_Wheels" title="Wagon Wheels">Wagon Wheels</a> (with another main factory in <a href="/wiki/Torfaen" title="Torfaen">Torfaen</a>, south Wales); it is the UK\'s second largest biscuit maker and was founded in Blackpool.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Crown_Paints" title="Crown Paints">Crown Paints</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Darwen" title="Darwen">Darwen</a> (500).<sup id="cite_ref-LTRecr_49-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTRecr-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/DS_Smith" title="DS Smith">DS Smith</a> have the Hollins paper mill just south of junction 4 of the M65, off the A666 in Darwen, which is set to close. Across the M65 to the north <a href="/wiki/Apeks" title="Apeks">Apeks</a> make <a href="/wiki/Diving_equipment" title="Diving equipment">diving equipment</a> at <a href="/wiki/Blackamoor,_Lancashire" title="Blackamoor, Lancashire">Blackamoor</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Graham_%26_Brown&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Graham &amp; Brown (page does not exist)">Graham &amp; Brown</a> at Blackburn make fancy wallpaper, next to the Leeds &amp; Liverpool Canal, and off the A6077 is <a href="/w/index.php?title=CWV_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="CWV (company) (page does not exist)">CWV</a> (<a href="/wiki/Coloroll" title="Coloroll">Coloroll</a> and <a href="/wiki/Crown_Wallpaper" title="Crown Wallpaper">Crown Wallpaper</a>); <a href="/wiki/Capita_Group" class="mw-redirect" title="Capita Group">Capita Group</a> runs <a href="/wiki/Television_licensing_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Television licensing in the United Kingdom">TV Licensing</a> in the middle of the town; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lucite_International&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lucite International (page does not exist)">Lucite International</a> has its main plant on the A666 in the north of the town centre, where it makes <a href="/wiki/Lucite" class="mw-redirect" title="Lucite">Lucite</a>; this site, under ICI Acrylics, manufactured the <a href="/wiki/Perspex" class="mw-redirect" title="Perspex">perspex</a> for wartime aircraft canopies from 1940, becoming Ineos Acrylics from 1999 until 2002 and the company is the world\'s largest manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Methyl_methacrylate" title="Methyl methacrylate">methyl methacrylate</a> (MMA); <a href="/w/index.php?title=ICI_Acrylics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ICI Acrylics (page does not exist)">ICI Acrylics</a> invented the process to make perspex in 1936; the granular form of Perspex was known by ICI as Leukon. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Tensar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tensar (page does not exist)">Tensar International</a>, invented and manufacture <a href="/wiki/Geogrid" title="Geogrid">geogrids</a> for construction, off the A6077 near junction 5 of the M65 in Blackburn near the B6231 roundabout; nearby is <a href="/w/index.php?title=A._M._Castle_%26_Co.&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="A. M. Castle &amp; Co. (page does not exist)">Castle Metals</a> UK; also on the Shadsworth Business Park is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Evertaut&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Evertaut (page does not exist)">Evertaut</a>, who make <a href="/wiki/Auditorium" title="Auditorium">auditorium</a> seating.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Greater_Manchester">Greater Manchester</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Greater Manchester">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Greater_Manchester#Economy" title="Greater Manchester">Greater Manchester \xc2\xa7&#160;Economy</a></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Manchester" title="Economy of Manchester">Economy of Manchester</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_companies_based_in_Greater_Manchester" title="List of companies based in Greater Manchester">List of companies based in Greater Manchester</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Liverpool%E2%80%93Manchester_rivalry" title="Liverpool\xe2\x80\x93Manchester rivalry">Liverpool\xe2\x80\x93Manchester rivalry</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Tyco_International" title="Tyco International">Tyco</a> UK is based on the A62 in <a href="/wiki/Newton_Heath" title="Newton Heath">Newton Heath</a>. <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Holt%27s_Brewery" title="Joseph Holt&#39;s Brewery">Joseph Holt\'s Brewery</a> is off the A665 next to <a href="/wiki/Manchester_(HM_Prison)" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester (HM Prison)">Strangeways prison</a>; <a href="/wiki/Boddingtons" class="mw-redirect" title="Boddingtons">Boddingtons</a>\' <a href="/wiki/Strangeways_Brewery" title="Strangeways Brewery">Strangeways Brewery</a> closed in 2006. <a href="/wiki/Avecia" title="Avecia">Avecia</a> (biotechnology) is off the A664 in the Hexagon Tower in <a href="/wiki/Blackley" title="Blackley">Blackley</a> near the <a href="/wiki/North_Manchester_General_Hospital" title="North Manchester General Hospital">North Manchester General Hospital</a>. North of the hospital at <a href="/wiki/Crumpsall" title="Crumpsall">Crumpsall</a> was <a href="/w/index.php?title=B3_Cable_Solutions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="B3 Cable Solutions (page does not exist)">B3 Cable Solutions</a>, the UK\'s only former manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Telecommunications_cable" title="Telecommunications cable">telecommunications cables</a>, based next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Irk" title="River Irk">River Irk</a>. Heineken (former <a href="/wiki/Scottish_%26_Newcastle" title="Scottish &amp; Newcastle">Scottish &amp; Newcastle</a>) have their large Royal Brewery in Moss Side next to the A5103, north of the B5219 junction. <a href="/wiki/Admiral_Sportswear" title="Admiral Sportswear">Admiral Sportswear</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Northenden" title="Northenden">Northenden</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Textile_Technology_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="British Textile Technology Group (page does not exist)">British Textile Technology Group</a> is in Didsbury. <a href="/wiki/Timpson_(retailer)" title="Timpson (retailer)">Timpson</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Wythenshawe" title="Wythenshawe">Wythenshawe</a>; <a href="/wiki/Sharwood%27s" title="Sharwood&#39;s">Sharwood\'s</a> used to make their sauces there until Premier Foods moved production to <a href="/wiki/Bury_St_Edmunds" title="Bury St Edmunds">Bury St Edmunds</a> in 2008. <a href="/wiki/Duerr%27s" class="mw-redirect" title="Duerr&#39;s">Duerr\'s</a> make honey and jam at the Roundthorn Ind Estate in Wythenshawe, off the <a href="/wiki/A560_road" title="A560 road">A560</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Shell_UK" class="mw-redirect" title="Shell UK">Shell UK</a> (retail) was at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Rowlandsway_House&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rowlandsway House (page does not exist)">Rowlandsway House</a> in Wythenshawe until 2011 and has moved to Brabazon House nearby on the Concord Business Park; <a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_Shell" title="Royal Dutch Shell">Royal Dutch Shell</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_largest_companies_by_revenue" title="List of largest companies by revenue">by revenue</a> ($458bn) in 2010, was the world\'s largest company, with <a href="/wiki/ExxonMobil" title="ExxonMobil">ExxonMobil</a> second. Electrium make their Wylex <a href="/wiki/Distribution_board" title="Distribution board">fuse boxes</a> on the B5168 and B5166 in Wythenshawe, north of the <a href="/wiki/Sharston" title="Sharston">Sharston</a> Interchange of the M56; to the west is a plant of the <a href="/wiki/Heimbach_Group" title="Heimbach Group">Heimbach Group</a>. <a href="/wiki/PZ_Cussons" title="PZ Cussons">PZ Cussons</a> (formerly in <a href="/wiki/Cheadle_Heath" title="Cheadle Heath">Cheadle Heath</a>) is off the Airport Interchange of the M56, with a manufacturing site on the former <a href="/wiki/Agecroft_Colliery" title="Agecroft Colliery">Agecroft Colliery</a> next to the <a href="/wiki/Ribble_Valley_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Ribble Valley Line">railway</a> in Pendlebury, Salford, off the A6044. Nearby in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Moss_Nook&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Moss Nook (page does not exist)">Moss Nook</a> is <a href="/wiki/Franke_(company)" title="Franke (company)">Franke UK</a>, the world\'s largest manufacturer of domestic <a href="/wiki/Sink" title="Sink">sinks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Simon_Carves" title="Simon Carves">Simon Carves</a> (<a href="/wiki/Process_engineering" title="Process engineering">process engineering</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Renold" class="mw-redirect" title="Renold">Renold plc</a> is an international chain company based on the B5166, off the Manchester Airport spur of the M56. Amazon have a <a href="/wiki/Fulfillment_house" title="Fulfillment house">fulfilment centre</a> off the A538 west of the airport, south of the Hale Four Seasons Roundabout of the M56.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/N_Brown_Group" title="N Brown Group">N Brown Group</a> (JD Williams) is one of Britain\'s main clothing manufacturers and retailers, and based in\ncentral Manchester near the A62/A665 junction and Sir <a href="/wiki/Owen_Williams_(engineer)" title="Owen Williams (engineer)">Owen William</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/Daily_Express_Building,_Manchester" title="Daily Express Building, Manchester">Daily Express Building</a>, and owns well-known brands. <a href="/wiki/Gazprom" title="Gazprom">Gazprom Energy</a> is on <a href="/wiki/Quay_Street" title="Quay Street">Quay Street</a> (A34) towards the River Irwell.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg/220px-Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg/330px-Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg/440px-Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="427" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Heinz_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1224705.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/H._J._Heinz_Company" class="mw-redirect" title="H. J. Heinz Company">Heinz</a>, although based in <a href="/wiki/Hayes,_Hillingdon" title="Hayes, Hillingdon">Hayes</a> in <a href="/wiki/Middlesex" title="Middlesex">Middlesex</a>, has the <a href="/wiki/H._J._Heinz,_Wigan" title="H. J. Heinz, Wigan">largest food processing complex</a> in Europe at a 55-acre (220,000&#160;m<sup>2</sup>) site at <a href="/wiki/Kitt_Green" title="Kitt Green">Kitt Green</a> in Wigan, which produces 1.4 billion cans of food each year; it is accessed to the east of the <a href="/wiki/Orrell,_Greater_Manchester" title="Orrell, Greater Manchester">Orrell</a> Interchange of the M6 (<a href="/wiki/A577_road" title="A577 road">A577</a>); the 38-acre Heinz NDC is next door</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/JJB_Sports" title="JJB Sports">JJB Sports</a> is at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Marsh_Green,_Wigan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Marsh Green, Wigan (page does not exist)">Marsh Green</a> near the <a href="/wiki/River_Douglas_(Lancashire)" title="River Douglas (Lancashire)">River Douglas</a>, set up by former footballer <a href="/wiki/Dave_Whelan" title="Dave Whelan">Dave Whelan</a> who owns <a href="/wiki/Wigan_Athletic_F.C." title="Wigan Athletic F.C.">Wigan Athletic F.C.</a>; also in Wigan are <a href="/wiki/The_Tote" title="The Tote">The Tote</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Shearings_Holidays&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Shearings Holidays (page does not exist)">Shearings Holidays</a> and <a href="/wiki/Girobank" title="Girobank">Girobank</a>, and <a href="/wiki/R%26R_Ice_Cream" title="R&amp;R Ice Cream">R&amp;R Ice Cream</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Richmond_Foods" class="mw-redirect" title="Richmond Foods">Richmond Foods</a>) make <a href="/w/index.php?title=De_Roma&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="De Roma (page does not exist)">De Roma</a> ice cream. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Contitech&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Contitech (page does not exist)">Contitech</a> UK (part of Continental AG) makes industrial <a href="/wiki/Belt_(mechanical)" title="Belt (mechanical)">belts</a> off the <a href="/wiki/A587_road" title="A587 road">A587</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bickershaw" title="Bickershaw">Bickershaw</a>, between Wigan and Leigh. Bulldog Tools make <a href="/wiki/Spade" title="Spade">spades</a> on the A577 in the east of Wigan. <a href="/wiki/Electrium" title="Electrium">Electrium</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=Volex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Volex (page does not exist)">Volex</a>) make <a href="/wiki/Electrical_wiring_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Electrical wiring in the United Kingdom">electrical wiring</a> off the A578, north of <a href="/wiki/Westleigh,_Greater_Manchester" title="Westleigh, Greater Manchester">Westleigh</a>. Ainscough Crane Hire is the UK\'s largest lifting services company on Bradley Hall Est in <a href="/wiki/Standish,_Greater_Manchester" title="Standish, Greater Manchester">Standish</a>, next to the WCML. Off the A580 at the <a href="/wiki/A573_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A573 road">A573</a> roundabout at <a href="/wiki/Golborne" title="Golborne">Golborne</a>, at Stone Cross Park south of the borough, is <a href="/wiki/Alpla" title="Alpla">Alpla</a> UK (plastic bottles) and <a href="/wiki/Sofology" title="Sofology">Sofology</a> (furniture).\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Makro" title="Makro">Makro</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Eccles,_Greater_Manchester" title="Eccles, Greater Manchester">Eccles</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Akcros_Chemicals&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Akcros Chemicals (page does not exist)">Akcros Chemicals</a> are off the A576. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cooper_%26_Stollbrand&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cooper &amp; Stollbrand (page does not exist)">Cooper &amp; Stollbrand</a> make premium garments next to the River Irwell on Cambridge Ind Est in <a href="/wiki/Broughton,_Greater_Manchester" class="mw-redirect" title="Broughton, Greater Manchester">Lower Broughton</a>. On the Bolton boundary in north of the borough in <a href="/wiki/Little_Hulton" title="Little Hulton">Little Hulton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eaton_Corporation" title="Eaton Corporation">Eaton Transmissions</a> closed in 2006, with production moving to <a href="/wiki/Tczew" title="Tczew">Tczew</a> in Poland. class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester Docks">Pomona Docks</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ordsall,_Greater_Manchester" title="Ordsall, Greater Manchester">Ordsall</a>. <a href="/wiki/Pentair" 2006</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Sock_Shop" title="Sock Shop">Sock Shop</a> is in Bolton, and <a href="/wiki/MBDA" title="MBDA">MBDA</a> (<a href="/wiki/Matra" title="Matra">Matra</a> <a href="/wiki/BAe_Dynamics" title="BAe Dynamics">BAe Dynamics</a> <a href="/wiki/Alenia_Marconi_Systems" title="Alenia Marconi Systems">Alenia</a>, owned 37.5% by BAE Systems) makes missiles in <a href="/wiki/Lostock,_Bolton" title="Lostock, Bolton">Lostock</a> near the Horwich Link Interchange of the M61; it is the historic main manufacturing site of Britain\'s aircraft-launched missiles; MBDA Lostock is MBDA\'s largest production site (of the whole company) and makes the air-to-air <a href="/wiki/ASRAAM" title="ASRAAM">ASRAAM</a> (found on the Eurofighter) and the air-to-surface <a href="/wiki/Active_radar_homing" title="Active radar homing">active radar homing</a> <a href="/wiki/Brimstone_(missile)" title="Brimstone (missile)">Brimstone (missile)</a> designed by GEC-Marconi in the 1990s, and previously made the <a href="/wiki/Rapier_(missile)" title="Rapier (missile)">Rapier</a> <a href="/wiki/Surface-to-air_missile" title="Surface-to-air missile">surface-to-air missile</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/De_Havilland_Firestreak" title="De Havilland Firestreak">De Havilland Firestreak</a>, Britain\'s first (<a href="/wiki/Infrared_homing" title="Infrared homing">infrared homing</a>) <a href="/wiki/Air-to-air_missile" title="Air-to-air missile">air-to-air missile</a>. <a href="/wiki/Cash_Generator" title="Cash Generator">Cash Generator</a> is south of the borough off the <a href="/wiki/A575_road" title="A575 road">A575</a> in <a href="/wiki/Farnworth" title="Farnworth">Farnworth</a>, north of the Salford boundary; <a Gate">Moses Gate</a>, in East Farnworth. <a href="/wiki/Dabs.com" title="Dabs.com">dabs.com</a>, an e-commerce site owned by BT, is in <a href="/wiki/Wingates" title="Wingates">Wingates</a> (<a next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Croal" title="River Croal">River Croal</a> off the A58 at <a href="/wiki/Tonge,_Greater_Manchester" title="Tonge, Greater Manchester">Tonge Moor</a> next to <a around the UK, such as <a href="/wiki/Aspire_(sculpture)" title="Aspire (sculpture)">Aspire</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Clyde_Arc" title="Clyde Arc">Clyde Arc</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems"
