class="mw-redirect" title="Dane Road Metrolink station">Dane Road Metrolink station</a> in Sale. <a href="/w/index.php?title=S2Blue&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="S2Blue (page does not exist)">S2Blue</a>, a radio jingles company run by <a href="/wiki/Steve_England" title="Steve England">Steve England</a>, is off the A6144 near the B5165 junction, in <a href="/wiki/Ashton_upon_Mersey" title="Ashton upon Mersey">Ashton upon Mersey</a> in the former studios of <a href="/wiki/Alfasound" title="Alfasound">Alfasound</a> (having moved from <a href="/wiki/Leek,_Staffordshire" title="Leek, Staffordshire">Leek</a> in 2013). <a href="/wiki/HomeForm_Group" title="HomeForm Group">HomeForm Group</a>, owner of <a href="/wiki/Moben_Kitchens" class="mw-redirect" title="Moben Kitchens">M\xc3\xb6ben Kitchens</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sharps_Bedrooms" title="Sharps Bedrooms">Sharps Bedrooms</a> and Dolphin Bathrooms until 2011, was on the <a href="/wiki/A56_road" title="A56 road">A56</a> in <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford_(district)" title="Old Trafford (district)">Old Trafford</a>. <a href="/wiki/Itron" title="Itron">Itron</a> UK (flow metering) have a plant at the A56/A5014 junction at <a href="/wiki/Gorse_Hill" title="Gorse Hill">Gorse Hillin</a> Stretford; further along the A5014 there is Kelloggs UK HQ next to the Old Trafford cricket ground. <a href="/wiki/Regatta_(clothing)" title="Regatta (clothing)">Regatta</a> and <a href="/wiki/Craghoppers" title="Craghoppers">Craghoppers</a> are on Barton Dock Road (B5211), near the <a href="/wiki/Trafford_Centre" title="Trafford Centre">Trafford Centre</a> (the base of <a href="/wiki/The_Peel_Group" title="The Peel Group">The Peel Group</a>), on the other side of the A5081. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Holt_Lloyd&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Holt Lloyd (page does not exist)">Holt Lloyd</a>, known as Holts, the largest car care company in the world in the 1980s, now owned by Honeywell Consumer Products Group, is based on Barton Dock Road (B5211), at Merlin Park on the south of Trafford Park, off the M60 Lostock Circle. On Trafford Park near the A576 <a href="/w/index.php?title=Centenary_Bridge_(Manchester)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Centenary Bridge (Manchester) (page does not exist)">Centenary Bridge</a> <a href="/wiki/Svenska_Cellulosa_Aktiebolaget" class="mw-redirect" title="Svenska Cellulosa Aktiebolaget">SCA</a> makes household tissue products (owned by <a href="/wiki/Procter_%26_Gamble" title="Procter &amp; Gamble">P&amp;G</a> before 2007), and next door is P&amp;G\'s Manchester Plant which makes its <i><a href="/wiki/Pampers" title="Pampers">Pampers</a></i> nappies. <a href="/w/index.php?title=The_Fragrance_Shop&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="The Fragrance Shop (page does not exist)">The Fragrance Shop</a> is based near <a href="/w/index.php?title=Trafford_Ecology_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Trafford Ecology Park (page does not exist)">Trafford Ecology Park</a>, on Trafford Park. <a href="/wiki/Soreen" title="Soreen">Soreen</a> is made south of Trafford Park, next to the Bridgewater Canal off the A5081 Parkway Circle roundabout; next door UK Data Capture (Lockheed Martin) processed all the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Census_2011" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom Census 2011">2011</a> Census data.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg/220px-The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg/330px-The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg/440px-The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Best_to_You_Each_Morning%5E_-_geograph.org.uk_-_47831.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kelloggs in Manchester, looking north along the A5181 next to <a href="/wiki/Greater_Manchester_Fire_and_Rescue_Service" title="Greater Manchester Fire and Rescue Service">GMFRS</a>\'s Stretford Area Command HQ; the site is the largest producer of cereals in Europe</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Kelloggs" class="mw-redirect" title="Kelloggs">Kelloggs</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Trafford_Park" title="Trafford Park">Trafford Park</a> (Manchester); to the north Adidas have their European distribution centre, and nearby <a href="/wiki/TDG_Limited" title="TDG Limited">TDG</a> was on the industrial estate, until bought by <a href="/wiki/Norbert_Dentressangle" title="Norbert Dentressangle">Norbert Dentressangle</a> in 2011. <a href="/wiki/DHL_Freight" title="DHL Freight">DHL Freight</a> UK is at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Manchester_International_Freight_Terminal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Manchester International Freight Terminal (page does not exist)">Manchester International Freight Terminal</a>, west of the Old Trafford football ground. <a href="/wiki/Chemtura" title="Chemtura">Chemtura</a> (chemicals, former site of <a href="/wiki/Ciba-Geigy" class="mw-redirect" title="Ciba-Geigy">Ciba-Geigy</a>) is between the A576 and B5214 towards the north end of the industrial park. <a href="/wiki/Lucchini_RS" title="Lucchini RS">Lucchini</a> UK (railway <a href="/wiki/Wheelset_(rail_transport)" title="Wheelset (rail transport)">wheelsets</a> and axles) are on Trafford Park off the B5214, and are a main supplier for UK trains. <a href="/wiki/Ocean_Finance" title="Ocean Finance">Ocean Finance</a> is on Trafford Park (previously in <a href="/wiki/Tamworth,_Staffordshire" title="Tamworth, Staffordshire">Tamworth</a>). <a href="/wiki/Hot_Animation" title="Hot Animation">Hot Animation</a>, who made <i><a href="/wiki/Bob_the_Builder" title="Bob the Builder">Bob the Builder</a></i>, are on Hanover Business Park in the east of Altrincham, in <a href="/wiki/Broadheath,_Greater_Manchester" title="Broadheath, Greater Manchester">Broadheath</a>; to the south towards the Bridgewater Canal, across a <a href="/wiki/Warrington_and_Altrincham_Junction_Railway" title="Warrington and Altrincham Junction Railway">former railway</a>, on the Altrincham Ind Est, <a href="/wiki/Girlguiding" title="Girlguiding">Girlguiding</a> UK run their trading service.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:JD_Sports,_Belfast,_March_2011.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/JD_Sports%2C_Belfast%2C_March_2011.JPG/150px-JD_Sports%2C_Belfast%2C_March_2011.JPG" width="150" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/JD_Sports%2C_Belfast%2C_March_2011.JPG/225px-JD_Sports%2C_Belfast%2C_March_2011.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/JD_Sports%2C_Belfast%2C_March_2011.JPG/300px-JD_Sports%2C_Belfast%2C_March_2011.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2848" data-file-height="4272" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:JD_Sports,_Belfast,_March_2011.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>JD Sports (in Belfast), the largest company in Bury</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/JD_Sports" title="JD Sports">JD Sports</a> is west of the <a href="/wiki/Pilsworth" title="Pilsworth">Pilsworth</a> Interchange of the M66 in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hollins,_Bury&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hollins, Bury (page does not exist)">Hollins</a> south of <a href="/wiki/Bury,_Greater_Manchester" title="Bury, Greater Manchester">Bury</a>; <a href="/wiki/Birthdays_(retailer)" title="Birthdays (retailer)">Birthdays</a> is west of the Heap Bridge Interchange; Tetrosyl Group Ltd, UK maker of car care products are at <a href="/wiki/Walmersley" title="Walmersley">Walmersley</a>, off the A56 and also at junction 2 (A58) of the M66. At A6053/A56 junction in <a href="/wiki/Redvales" title="Redvales">Redvales</a>, to the south of Bury is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Swintex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Swintex (page does not exist)">Melba Swintex</a>, a main supplier of <a href="/wiki/Street_furniture" title="Street furniture">street furniture</a>\xe2\x80\x94<a href="/wiki/Traffic_cone" title="Traffic cone">traffic cones</a> and <a href="/wiki/Traffic_barrier" title="Traffic barrier">barriers</a>, claiming to be a world leader. <a href="/wiki/Milliken_%26_Company" title="Milliken &amp; Company">Milliken</a> make airbags on the A58, south-west of Bury.\n</p><p>PTG (Holroyd Machine Tools) are based off the M62 <a href="/wiki/Milnrow" title="Milnrow">Milnrow</a> Interchange; nearby off the A6193 are <a href="/wiki/Takeuchi_Manufacturing" title="Takeuchi Manufacturing">Takeuchi Manufacturing</a> UK (construction equipment). <a href="/wiki/Premier_Foods" title="Premier Foods">Premier Foods</a> make <a href="/wiki/Sarson%27s" title="Sarson&#39;s">Sarson\'s</a> on the A669 near <a href="/wiki/Mills_Hill_railway_station" title="Mills Hill railway station">Mills Hill railway station</a> in <a href="/wiki/Middleton,_Greater_Manchester" title="Middleton, Greater Manchester">Middleton</a>; on the opposite side of the railway <a href="/w/index.php?title=Vita_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Vita Group (page does not exist)">Vita Group</a> make <a href="/wiki/List_of_polyurethane_applications" title="List of polyurethane applications">polyurethane foam</a> (Vitafoam, the largest supplier in the UK). Voith Paper have a servicing centre on the <a href="/wiki/A576_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A576 road">A576</a>, west of Middleton town centre. The <a href="/wiki/Co-op_UK" class="mw-redirect" title="Co-op UK">Co-op</a> is based in Manchester and <a href="/wiki/Rochdale" title="Rochdale">Rochdale</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Minky_Homecare&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Minky Homecare (page does not exist)">Minky Homecare</a> (<a href="/wiki/Housekeeping" title="Housekeeping">household cleaning</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Freudenberg_Group" title="Freudenberg Group">Freudenberg Household Products</a> UK is in the centre of Rochdale off the <a href="/wiki/A671_road" title="A671 road">A671</a>. Zen Internet is at Sandbrook House on <a href="/w/index.php?title=Sandbrook_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sandbrook Park (page does not exist)">Sandbrook Park</a> at end of the <a href="/wiki/A627(M)_motorway" title="A627(M) motorway">A627(M)</a> off the A664 in Stoneyfield in the south of Rochdale, and next door is the HQ of <a href="/wiki/The_Co-operative_Pharmacy" class="mw-redirect" title="The Co-operative Pharmacy">The Co-operative Pharmacy</a>. <a href="/wiki/We_Buy_Any_Car" title="We Buy Any Car">We Buy Any Car</a> is at <a href="/wiki/Castleton,_Greater_Manchester" title="Castleton, Greater Manchester">Castleton</a> near the A664, in the south-west of Rochdale, the same site of <a href="/wiki/Carcraft" title="Carcraft">Carcraft</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=C.H._Guenther&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="C.H. Guenther (page does not exist)">Guenther Bakeries</a> (owned by Golden West, part of RHM, until 2005) in the south of Heywood, east of the large Heywood Distribution Park, makes the bread buns for <a href="/wiki/McDonald%27s" title="McDonald&#39;s">McDonald\'s</a> (with another site in Banbury).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Merseyside">Merseyside</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Merseyside">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Merseyside#Economy" title="Merseyside">Merseyside \xc2\xa7&#160;Economy</a></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Liverpool" title="Economy of Liverpool">Economy of Liverpool</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Littlewoods_Building.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Littlewoods_Building.jpg/220px-Littlewoods_Building.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Littlewoods_Building.jpg/330px-Littlewoods_Building.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/Littlewoods_Building.jpg/440px-Littlewoods_Building.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Littlewoods_Building.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The 1938 <a href="/wiki/Littlewoods_Pools_building" title="Littlewoods Pools building">Littlewood\'s Building</a> next to <a href="/wiki/Wavertree_Technology_Park" title="Wavertree Technology Park">Wavertree Technology Park</a>, on <a href="/wiki/Edge_Lane" title="Edge Lane">Edge Lane</a>, looking east from <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Cathedral" title="Liverpool Cathedral">Liverpool Cathedral</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Pilkington" title="Pilkington">Pilkington</a> is in <a href="/wiki/St_Helens,_Merseyside" title="St Helens, Merseyside">St. Helens</a>; <a href="/wiki/Knauf_Insulation" title="Knauf Insulation">Knauf Insulation</a> UK, is south-west of the town centre. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Alumasc&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Alumasc (page does not exist)">Alumasc</a> Exterior Building Products is on B5204 near <a href="/wiki/St_Helens_Junction_railway_station" title="St Helens Junction railway station">St Helens Junction railway station</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sutton,_St_Helens" title="Sutton, St Helens">Sutton</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Kalzip&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Kalzip (page does not exist)">Kalzip</a>, a division of <a href="/wiki/Tata_Steel_Europe" title="Tata Steel Europe">Tata Steel Europe</a>, make aluminium roofs in <a href="/wiki/Haydock" title="Haydock">Haydock</a>; <a href="/wiki/Gas_Control_Equipment_Ltd" title="Gas Control Equipment Ltd">GCE Group</a> UK, who make <a href="/wiki/Medical_gas_supply" title="Medical gas supply">medical gas controllers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diving_regulator" title="Diving regulator">diving regulators</a>, are on the <a href="/wiki/A599_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A599 road">A599</a> near the M6 Haydock Island; to the north-west is a large Sainsbury\'s RDC; further up the A49 before Ashton-in-Makerfield and <a href="/wiki/Byrchall_High_School" title="Byrchall High School">Byrchall High School</a> is <a href="/wiki/Speedy_Hire" title="Speedy Hire">Speedy Hire</a>, the biggest hire firm in the UK. <a href="/wiki/Vimto" title="Vimto">Vimto</a> is owned by <a href="/wiki/Nichols_plc" title="Nichols plc">Nichols plc</a> of <a href="/wiki/Newton-le-Willows" title="Newton-le-Willows">Newton-le-Willows</a>, although actually made by <a href="/wiki/Cott" title="Cott">Cott Beverages</a> in north <a href="/wiki/Leicestershire" title="Leicestershire">Leicestershire</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Littlewoods" title="Littlewoods">Littlewoods</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Garston,_Merseyside" class="mw-redirect" title="Garston, Merseyside">Garston</a>, who are owned by the <a href="/wiki/Shop_Direct_Group" class="mw-redirect" title="Shop Direct Group">Shop Direct Group</a> in <a href="/wiki/Speke" title="Speke">Speke</a>. <a href="/wiki/Princes_(company)" class="mw-redirect" title="Princes (company)">Princes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Johnsons_Cleaners_UK" title="Johnsons Cleaners UK">Johnsons Cleaners UK</a>, <a href="/wiki/A._P._Moller-Maersk_Group" class="mw-redirect" title="A. P. Moller-Maersk Group">Maersk Line UK</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Beetham_Organization" title="Beetham Organization">Beetham Organization</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_West_Foods" title="John West Foods">John West Foods</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bibby_Line" title="Bibby Line">Bibby Line</a>, <a href="/wiki/Home_Bargains" title="Home Bargains">Home Bargains</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Liver_Friendly_Society" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Liver Friendly Society">Royal Liver Assurance</a> and <a href="/wiki/T_J_Hughes" class="mw-redirect" title="T J Hughes">T J Hughes</a> have their headquarters in Liverpool. Towards <a href="/wiki/Aintree" title="Aintree">Aintree</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s" title="Jacob&#39;s">Jacob\'s</a> and their crackers are historically based, and also make <a href="/wiki/Twiglets" title="Twiglets">Twiglets</a> at their site at <a href="/wiki/Hartley%27s" title="Hartley&#39;s">Hartley\'s</a> Village in <a href="/wiki/Fazakerley" title="Fazakerley">Fazakerley</a>, and nearby is <a href="/wiki/Sportech_PLC" class="mw-redirect" title="Sportech PLC">Sportech PLC</a>, owner of the <a href="/wiki/Football_pool" class="mw-redirect" title="Football pool">football pools</a>; Trigon Snacks make <a href="/wiki/Big_D_(peanuts)" title="Big D (peanuts)">Big D (peanuts)</a> in Aintree, and have done since the 1970s on the Greylaw Ind Est off the B5187, near the <a href="/wiki/Archbishop_Beck_Catholic_Sports_College" title="Archbishop Beck Catholic Sports College">Archbishop Beck Catholic Sports College</a>. HMRC\'s (former Inland Revenue) <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Insolvency_Unit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="National Insolvency Unit (page does not exist)">National Insolvency Unit</a> is at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Regian_House&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Regian House (page does not exist)">Regian House</a> (previously at <a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Dock,_Port_of_Liverpool" title="Queen&#39;s Dock, Port of Liverpool">Queen\'s Dock</a>) opposite <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_James_Street_railway_station" title="Liverpool James Street railway station">Liverpool James Street railway station</a> and next to Liverpool\'s <a href="/w/index.php?title=Armed_Forces_Careers_Office&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Armed Forces Careers Office (page does not exist)">Armed Forces Careers Office</a>. The Criminal Records Bureau is on <a href="/wiki/Prince%27s_Dock,_Liverpool" title="Prince&#39;s Dock, Liverpool">Prince\'s Dock</a>, since 2013 part of the new <a href="/wiki/Disclosure_and_Barring_Service" title="Disclosure and Barring Service">Disclosure and Barring Service</a> (with the former <a href="/wiki/Independent_Safeguarding_Authority" title="Independent Safeguarding Authority">ISA</a> in Darlington). The <a href="/wiki/Defence_Bills_Agency" title="Defence Bills Agency">Defence Bills Agency</a> was at Mersey House next to St James railway station, now part of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Business_Services" title="Defence Business Services">DBS Finance</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Tangerine_Confectionery" title="Tangerine Confectionery">Tangerine Confectionery</a> makes its Princess <a href="/wiki/Marshmallow" title="Marshmallow">marshmallows</a> off <a href="/wiki/Edge_Lane" title="Edge Lane">Edge Lane</a> (A5047) in east Liverpool, west of Wavertree Technology Park. <a href="/wiki/Home_Bargains" title="Home Bargains">Home Bargains</a> are off the <a href="/wiki/A580_road" title="A580 road">A580</a> west of junction 4 of the M57, on the Knowsley boundary at <a href="/wiki/Stonebridge_Park,_Liverpool" title="Stonebridge Park, Liverpool">Stonebridge Park</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=JF_Renshaw&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="JF Renshaw (page does not exist)">JF Renshaw</a> (Renshaw Napier), who have a Royal warrant, make <a href="/wiki/Icing_(food)" title="Icing (food)">cake icing</a> on the <a href="/wiki/A562_road" title="A562 road">A562</a> next to the <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Women%27s_NHS_Foundation_Trust" title="Liverpool Women&#39;s NHS Foundation Trust">Liverpool Women\'s Hospital</a> in Edge Hill; 90% of the UK\'s <a href="/wiki/Marzipan" title="Marzipan">marzipan</a> comes from this factory. At Speke on the A561, west of the <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Land_Rover" title="Jaguar Land Rover">JLR</a> plant, partly in Knowsley, <a href="/wiki/Novartis" title="Novartis">Novartis</a> make vaccines such as <a href="/wiki/Influenza_vaccine" title="Influenza vaccine">Fluvirin</a>, and directly to the south <a href="/wiki/MedImmune" title="MedImmune">MedImmune</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/AstraZeneca" title="AstraZeneca">AstraZeneca</a>) makes components of influenza vaccine (<a href="/wiki/Live_attenuated_influenza_vaccine" title="Live attenuated influenza vaccine">FluMist</a>); <a href="/wiki/Briggs_Automotive_Company" title="Briggs Automotive Company">Briggs Automotive Company</a> is on Speke Hall Ind Est, with HP Chemie Pelzer UK (automobile <a href="/wiki/Absorption_(acoustics)" title="Absorption (acoustics)">acoustics</a>). At <a href="/wiki/Hunts_Cross" class="mw-redirect" title="Hunts Cross">Hunts Cross</a> on the northern side of the railway line, the large <a href="/wiki/Eli_Lilly_and_Company" title="Eli Lilly and Company">Eli Lilly</a> Speke Operations manufacturing plant produces antibiotics such as <a href="/wiki/Capreomycin" title="Capreomycin">Capreomycin</a>, and in 1981 produced the world\'s first <a href="/wiki/Biosynthesis" title="Biosynthesis">biosynthetic</a> product, by manufacturing <a href="/wiki/Biologic_medical_product" class="mw-redirect" title="Biologic medical product">biologic</a> insulin, and has also produced biosynthetic human <a href="/wiki/Growth_hormone" title="Growth hormone">growth hormone</a> since 1985; the plant was owned by <a href="/wiki/The_Distillers_Company" title="The Distillers Company">The Distillers Company</a> after the war until 1962, where it made penicillin and later made <a href="/wiki/Thalidomide" title="Thalidomide">thalidomide</a>. Near the A561/A562 junction, the <a href="/wiki/Northwest_Regional_Development_Agency" title="Northwest Regional Development Agency">NWDA</a>-funded <a href="/w/index.php?title=National_Biomanufacturing_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="National Biomanufacturing Centre (page does not exist)">National Biomanufacturing Centre</a> was built in 2006. On the south side of the A561 in Speke is Estuary Commerce Park. Further to south is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Prinovis&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Prinovis (page does not exist)">Prinovis</a> UK and <a href="/wiki/B_%26_M" title="B &amp; M">B &amp; M</a> (previously in Blackpool) on the Liverpool International Business Park; on the former Speke Aerodrome is <a href="/wiki/Shop_Direct" title="Shop Direct">Shop Direct</a> near the National Biomanufacturing Centre.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Entrance_to_Cereal_Partners_UK_factory,_Bromborough.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Entrance_to_Cereal_Partners_UK_factory%2C_Bromborough.jpg/220px-Entrance_to_Cereal_Partners_UK_factory%2C_Bromborough.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Entrance_to_Cereal_Partners_UK_factory%2C_Bromborough.jpg/330px-Entrance_to_Cereal_Partners_UK_factory%2C_Bromborough.jpg 1.5x, title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Cereal_Partners_Worldwide" title="Cereal Partners Worldwide">Cereal Partners</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Nestl%C3%A9" title="Nestl\xc3\xa9">Nestl\xc3\xa9</a>) make <a href="/wiki/Cheerios" title="Cheerios">Cheerios</a> and <a href="/wiki/Golden_Nuggets" title="Golden Nuggets">Golden Nuggets</a> on the A41 opposite Port Sunlight at <a href="/wiki/Bromborough" title="Bromborough">Bromborough</a>, also the base of <a href="/wiki/CSM_N.V." class="mw-redirect" title="CSM N.V.">CSM</a> UK, the baking ingredients company based at a former Unilever <a href="/wiki/Stork_(margarine)" title="Stork (margarine)">Stork</a> margarine site.</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Land_Rover" title="Jaguar Land Rover">Jaguar Land Rover</a> has 166 acres of its main <a href="/wiki/Halewood_Body_%26_Assembly" title="Halewood Body &amp; Assembly">production site</a> (formerly owned by <a href="/wiki/Ford_of_Europe" title="Ford of Europe">Ford</a>) in <a href="/wiki/Halewood" title="Halewood">Halewood</a>, making the <a href="/wiki/Land_Rover_Freelander" title="Land Rover Freelander">Freelander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Range_Rover_Evoque" title="Range Rover Evoque">Range Rover Evoque</a>. <a href="/wiki/Getrag" title="Getrag">Getrag Ford Transmissions</a>, make 400,000 <a href="/wiki/Automatic_transmission" title="Automatic transmission">automatic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manual_transmission" title="Manual transmission">manual transmissions</a> next door to the east of JLR\'s Halewood plant, for Ford, Volvo and Mazda vehicles. <a href="/wiki/Magna_International" title="Magna International">Magna Decoma</a>, west of JLR Halewood and east of Novartis, make car interiors and exteriors. <a href="/wiki/Dairy_Crest" title="Dairy Crest">Dairy Crest</a> makes <a href="/wiki/Vitalite" title="Vitalite">Vitalite</a> and <a href="/wiki/Utterly_Butterly" title="Utterly Butterly">Utterly Butterly</a> on the A5207 in <a href="/wiki/Kirkby" title="Kirkby">Kirkby</a>, off the M57 Randles Farm Interchange, opposite a former site of <a href="/wiki/Ethel_Austin" title="Ethel Austin">Ethel Austin</a>; to the east of Dairy Crest is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Yorkshire_Copper_Tube&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Yorkshire Copper Tube (page does not exist)">Yorkshire Copper Tube</a>, Britain\'s main manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Copper_tubing" title="Copper tubing">copper tubing</a>, owned by Italian <a href="/wiki/KME_Group" title="KME Group">KME Group</a>; Counterline make <a href="/wiki/Foodservice" title="Foodservice">foodservice</a> counters on Knowsley Business Park; <a href="/wiki/Clarke_Energy" title="Clarke Energy">Clarke Energy</a> is on the <a href="/wiki/A5208_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A5208 road">A5208</a>. Further north on the estate next to the A5208 is <a href="/wiki/QVC_(UK)" title="QVC (UK)">QVC UK</a>\'s distribution centre, with all three in Kirkby. Further north, next to the Lancashire boundary is Goodrich Actuation Systems on the Huyton Ind Est (in former Huyton Quarry) on the north-west side of the M62 <a href="/wiki/Tarbock_Island" class="mw-redirect" title="Tarbock Island">Tarbock Island</a> M62 (off the A5080) in <a href="/wiki/Tarbock" title="Tarbock">Tarbock</a>. Next door <a href="/wiki/Halewood_International" title="Halewood International">Halewood International</a>, who make <a href="/wiki/Lambrini" title="Lambrini">Lambrini</a>, Red Square, <a href="/wiki/Lamb%27s" title="Lamb&#39;s">Lamb\'s</a> Navy Rum and some <a href="/wiki/Alcopop" title="Alcopop">alcopops</a>, are in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Whitefield_Lane_End&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Whitefield Lane End (page does not exist)">Whitefield Lane End</a>, in the south of <a href="/wiki/Huyton" title="Huyton">Huyton</a> at the M62/M57 junction. Belling Ltd (owned by <a href="/wiki/Glen_Dimplex" class="mw-redirect" title="Glen Dimplex">Glen Dimplex</a>) is in <a href="/wiki/Whiston,_Merseyside" title="Whiston, Merseyside">Whiston</a>, next to the large <a href="/wiki/Whiston_Hospital" title="Whiston Hospital">Whiston Hospital</a>; Glen Dimplex Whiston is the UK\'s only manufacturer of cookers, around 350,000 a year (Stoves plc before 2001), and also owns <a href="/wiki/LEC_Refrigeration" title="LEC Refrigeration">LEC</a> fridges. Manesty manufactures medicine tablets off the B5194 on the Knowsley Business Park. Nationwide fashion retailer <a href="/wiki/Matalan" title="Matalan">Matalan</a> has its head office and main distribution centre in the north of the Knowsley Ind Est (at Skelmersdale until 2014); the Knowsley Ind Estate is all on the former <a href="/wiki/ROF_Kirkby" title="ROF Kirkby">ROF Kirkby</a>. <a href="/wiki/Camelot_Group" title="Camelot Group">Camelot Group</a> have their Liverpool Prize Payout Centre on the Kings Business Park on the A57, west of the M57 Forest House Interchange.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg/220px-Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg" width="220" height="151" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg/330px-Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg/440px-Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="439" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Unilever_Research_Laboratory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_524705.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Unilever_Research_%26_Development_Port_Sunlight_Laboratory" title="Unilever Research &amp; Development Port Sunlight Laboratory">Unilever Research Laboratory</a> at Port Sunlight (<a href="/wiki/Bebington" title="Bebington">Bebington</a>) looking west, next to the <a href="/wiki/Wirral_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Wirral Line">Wirral Line</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Typhoo" title="Typhoo">Typhoo</a> tea is made in <a href="/wiki/Moreton,_Merseyside" title="Moreton, Merseyside">Moreton</a> off the A551 next to <a href="/wiki/Moreton_(Merseyside)_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Moreton (Merseyside) railway station">Moreton railway station</a>, and on the same site there is Manor Bakeries (<a href="/wiki/Premier_Foods" title="Premier Foods">Premier Foods</a>, former <a href="/wiki/J._Lyons_and_Co." title="J. Lyons and Co.">Lyons Cakes</a>, before April 1995) who make <a href="/wiki/List_of_Cadbury_products" title="List of Cadbury products">mini rolls</a>, and a factory of <a href="/wiki/Burton%27s_Biscuit_Company" title="Burton&#39;s Biscuit Company">Burton\'s Biscuit Company</a> closed in December 2011 which made Cadbury\'s biscuits (<a href="/wiki/Cadbury_Fingers" title="Cadbury Fingers">Cadbury Fingers</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Wagon_Wheels" title="Wagon Wheels">Wagon Wheels</a>, where they still have a chocolate refinery. <a href="/wiki/Bristol-Myers_Squibb" title="Bristol-Myers Squibb">Bristol-Myers Squibb</a> UK have their main research laboratories east of the Moreton bakery, near <a href="/wiki/Leasowe_railway_station" title="Leasowe railway station">Leasowe railway station</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=CML_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="CML Group (page does not exist)">CML Group</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/Teledyne_Technologies" title="Teledyne Technologies">Teledyne</a>) makes composites and aircraft components off the A41 at Bromborough near <a href="/wiki/Eastham,_Merseyside" title="Eastham, Merseyside">Eastham Country Park</a>; to the south is <a href="/wiki/Einhell" title="Einhell">Einhell</a> UK (power tools). <a href="/wiki/Stiebel_Eltron" title="Stiebel Eltron">Stiebel Eltron</a> UK (heat pumps) nearby, are near <a href="/wiki/Meyer_Corporation" title="Meyer Corporation">Meyer</a> <a href="/w/index.php?title=Prestige_(cookware)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Prestige (cookware) (page does not exist)">Prestige</a> who make <a href="/wiki/Cookware_and_bakeware" title="Cookware and bakeware">cookware</a> (who also own <a href="/wiki/Circulon" title="Circulon">Circulon</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Anolon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Anolon (page does not exist)">Anolon</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Givaudan" title="Givaudan">Givaudan</a> UK have a fragrances factory. <a href="/wiki/Lithium_Corporation_of_America" title="Lithium Corporation of America">FMC Lithium</a>, east of the A41 at Wirral International Business Park, makes <a href="/wiki/Butyllithium" title="Butyllithium">butyllithium</a> and other <a href="/wiki/Organometallic_chemistry" title="Organometallic chemistry">organometallic</a> compounds. At <a href="/wiki/Port_Sunlight" title="Port Sunlight">Port Sunlight</a>, <a href="/wiki/Unilever" title="Unilever">Unilever</a> make and research detergents and shampoo, such as <i><a href="/wiki/Timotei" title="Timotei">Timotei</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Sunsilk" title="Sunsilk">Sunsilk</a></i>, as well as <i><a href="/wiki/Comfort_(fabric_softener)" title="Comfort (fabric softener)">Comfort</a></i> and <i>Persil Liquid</i>. <a href="/wiki/Cammell_Laird" title="Cammell Laird">Cammell Laird</a> at Birkenhead build ships, including two <a href="/wiki/UGM-27_Polaris" title="UGM-27 Polaris">Polaris</a> <a href="/wiki/Resolution-class_submarine" title="Resolution-class submarine">Resolution-class submarines</a> in the 1960s; on <a href="/wiki/Twelve_Quays" title="Twelve Quays">Twelve Quays</a> off the <a href="/wiki/A554_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A554 road">A554</a> is <a href="/wiki/Faiveley_Transport" title="Faiveley Transport">Faiveley Transport</a> UK (railway electrical components). <a href="/wiki/Survitec_Group" title="Survitec Group">RFD Beaufort</a> (known as Beaufort Air-Sea Equipment in the 1980s) make <a href="/wiki/G-suit" title="G-suit">G-suits</a> for <a href="/wiki/Fighter_aircraft" title="Fighter aircraft">fighter aircraft</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lifeboat_(shipboard)" title="Lifeboat (shipboard)">liferafts</a>. <a href="/wiki/Eastham_Oil_Terminal" title="Eastham Oil Terminal">Eastham Refinery</a> off junction 6 of the M53, at <a href="/wiki/Eastham,_Merseyside" title="Eastham, Merseyside">Eastham</a> in Wirral, just north of Hooton Park (in Cheshire), is owned by <a href="/wiki/Nynas" title="Nynas">Nynas</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:National_Girobank_(Alliance_and_Leicester)_HQ_-_geograph.org.uk_-_105597.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Former head office of the <a href="/wiki/Girobank" title="Girobank">Girobank</a> in Bootle; it closed in 2003; it was taken over by <a href="/wiki/Alliance_%26_Leicester" title="Alliance &amp; Leicester">Alliance &amp; Leicester</a> in 1990; it was established in Bootle in the late 1960s with help from Hugh Baird; it was the first financial institution in Europe to be fully computerised from the start</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Pontins" title="Pontins">Pontins</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Ainsdale" title="Ainsdale">Ainsdale</a>, Sefton. HMRC at <a href="/w/index.php?title=St_John%27s_House,_Bootle&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="St John&#39;s House, Bootle (page does not exist)">St John\'s House</a> on the A5057 in Bootle, is the national office for dealing with tax for <a href="/wiki/Individual_Savings_Account" title="Individual Savings Account">Individual Savings Accounts</a> (ISAs) and other savings schemes, charities (<a href="/wiki/Gift_Aid" title="Gift Aid">Gift Aid</a>), <a href="/w/index.php?title=Non-resident_trust&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Non-resident trust (page does not exist)">non-resident trusts</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Domicile_(law)" title="Domicile (law)">domicile</a> status; opposite is <a href="/wiki/Sefton_Metropolitan_Borough_Council" class="mw-redirect" title="Sefton Metropolitan Borough Council">Sefton Council</a>\'s Magdalen House. Nearby to the west on the A5057, the <a href="/wiki/Health_and_Safety_Executive" title="Health and Safety Executive">HSE</a> and <a href="/wiki/Office_for_Nuclear_Regulation" title="Office for Nuclear Regulation">Office for Nuclear Regulation</a> have their head office at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Redgrave_Court&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Redgrave Court (page does not exist)">Redgrave Court</a>, near the main site of <a href="/wiki/Hugh_Baird_College" title="Hugh Baird College">Hugh Baird College</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Inland_Revenue" title="Inland Revenue">Inland Revenue</a> had its main office at <a href="/w/index.php?title=The_Triad,_Bootle&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="The Triad, Bootle (page does not exist)">The Triad</a> in Bootle, next to the <a href="/wiki/New_Strand_Shopping_Centre" title="New Strand Shopping Centre">Strand Shopping Centre</a>, and the site is still run by HMRC. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Unipart_Dorman&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Unipart Dorman (page does not exist)">Unipart Dorman</a> make LED traffic lights near <a href="/wiki/Meols_Cop_railway_station" title="Meols Cop railway station">Meols Cop railway station</a> in <a href="/wiki/Blowick" title="Blowick">Blowick</a>, east of Southport; to the north at <a href="/wiki/Crossens" title="Crossens">Crossens</a>, <a href="/wiki/Railex" title="Railex">Railex</a> make <a href="/wiki/Filing_cabinet" title="Filing cabinet">filing cabinets</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cumbria_2">Cumbria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Cumbria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cumbria#Economy" title="Cumbria">Cumbria \xc2\xa7&#160;Economy</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> submarines and ships are made by <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Submarine_Solutions" class="mw-redirect" title="BAE Systems Submarine Solutions">BAE Systems Submarine Solutions</a> in <a href="/wiki/Barrow-in-Furness" title="Barrow-in-Furness">Barrow-in-Furness</a>. The coast of <a href="/wiki/Cumbria" title="Cumbria">Cumbria</a> is known as Britain\'s Energy Coast due to the large amounts of energy being produced along the coast of the county; <a href="/wiki/Sellafield" title="Sellafield">Sellafield</a> is a power station which is located in West Cumbria and is a major contributor to the "Energy Coast" also, <a href="/wiki/Barrow-in-Furness" title="Barrow-in-Furness">Barrow-in-Furness</a> is major town in contributing to the "Energy Coast" with a power station (<a href="/wiki/Roosecote_Power_Station" title="Roosecote Power Station">Roosecote Power Station</a>), Gas Terminals (<a href="/wiki/Rampside_Gas_Terminal" title="Rampside Gas Terminal">Rampside Gas Terminal</a>) and an offshore wind farm (<a href="/wiki/Walney_Wind_Farm" title="Walney Wind Farm">Walney Wind Farm</a>) which is approximately 14&#160;km (8.6 miles) west of the town\'s coastline with some of the largest wind turbines on Earth. On the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Westlakes_Science_%26_Technology_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Westlakes Science &amp; Technology Park (page does not exist)">Westlakes Science &amp; Technology Park</a> off the A595 south of Whitehaven, is the <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_Decommissioning_Authority" title="Nuclear Decommissioning Authority">Nuclear Decommissioning Authority</a> (in Herdus House).\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/British_Cattle_Movement_Service" title="British Cattle Movement Service">British Cattle Movement Service</a> is at Workington next to <a href="/wiki/Tata_Steel_Europe" title="Tata Steel Europe">Tata Steel Projects</a>, near a site of the <a href="/wiki/National_Nuclear_Laboratory" title="National Nuclear Laboratory">National Nuclear Laboratory</a> on Derwent Howe Ind Est. <a href="/wiki/Iggesund_Paperboard" title="Iggesund Paperboard">Iggesund Paperboard</a> is south of Workington, off the <a href="/wiki/A596_road" title="A596 road">A596</a>; next door is <a href="/wiki/Eastman_Chemical_Company" title="Eastman Chemical Company">Eastman Chemical</a>. <a href="/wiki/Amcor" title="Amcor">Amcor Flexibles Cumbria</a> (former Alcan before 2009) in the south of Workington prints <a href="/wiki/Potato_chip" title="Potato chip">crisp packets</a> and confectionery wrappers, for distribution around the UK\'s factories.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Lake_District" title="Lake District">Lake District</a> is popular with holiday makers. The <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_Decommissioning_Authority" title="Nuclear Decommissioning Authority">Nuclear Decommissioning Authority</a> is near Whitehaven. <a href="/wiki/Lakeland_(company)" title="Lakeland (company)">Lakeland</a>, who make kitchenware, are in Windermere. <a href="/wiki/Stobart_Group" title="Stobart Group">Stobart Group</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Carlisle,_Cumbria" class="mw-redirect" title="Carlisle, Cumbria">Carlisle</a>. <a href="/wiki/M-Sport" title="M-Sport">M-Sport</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Rallying" title="Rallying">rally team</a> at <a href="/wiki/Dovenby_Hall" title="Dovenby Hall">Dovenby Hall</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jennings_Brewery" title="Jennings Brewery">Jennings Brewery</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Cockermouth" title="Cockermouth">Cockermouth</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=James_Cropper_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="James Cropper (company) (page does not exist)">James Cropper</a>, Europe\'s leading manufacturer of coloured paper, is in <a href="/wiki/Burneside" title="Burneside">Burneside</a>, north of Kendal, on the <a href="/wiki/River_Kent" title="River Kent">River Kent</a> near the <a href="/wiki/A591_road" title="A591 road">A591</a>. Pirelli have their main UK tyre plant (for prestige cars) on the B5299 in south Carlisle; to the south in <a href="/wiki/Cummersdale" title="Cummersdale">Cummersdale</a> next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Caldew" title="River Caldew">River Caldew</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Stead_McAlpin&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Stead McAlpin (page does not exist)">Stead McAlpin</a> have a large textile site, formerly owned by <a href="/wiki/John_Lewis_Partnership" title="John Lewis Partnership">John Lewis</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=BSW_Timber&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="BSW Timber (page does not exist)">BSW Timber</a>, the UK\'s largest <a href="/wiki/Sawmill" title="Sawmill">sawmilling</a> company, has a large site north of Carlisle at <a href="/wiki/Cargo,_Cumbria" title="Cargo, Cumbria">Cargo</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kingmoor" title="Kingmoor">Kingmoor</a>, next to <a href="/wiki/Carlisle_Kingmoor_TMD" title="Carlisle Kingmoor TMD">Carlisle Kingmoor TMD</a> on the WCML. <a href="/wiki/BillerudKorsn%C3%A4s" title="BillerudKorsn\xc3\xa4s">BillerudKorsn\xc3\xa4s</a> had a paper mill at <a href="/wiki/Beetham" title="Beetham">Beetham</a> on the A6 next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Bela" title="River Bela">River Bela</a> in the south of the county. <a href="/wiki/Sealy_Corporation" title="Sealy Corporation">Sealy</a> UK make beds and mattresses on the B5031 next to <a href="/wiki/Aspatria_railway_station" title="Aspatria railway station">Aspatria railway station</a> in north Cumbria, west of Carlisle; next door <a href="/wiki/First_Milk_(company)" title="First Milk (company)">First Milk</a> make <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_District_Cheddar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lake District Cheddar (page does not exist)">Lake District Cheddar</a>. Further east along the A596, <a href="/wiki/Innovia_Films" title="Innovia Films">Innovia Films</a> (former British Rayophane) have a large site at <a href="/wiki/Wigton" title="Wigton">Wigton</a>. GSK Ulverston, built in 1949 as Glaxo to produce penicillin with a new plant to be built, makes <a href="/wiki/Cephalosporin" title="Cephalosporin">cephalosporin</a> antibiotics including <a href="/wiki/Cefuroxime" title="Cefuroxime">cefuroxime</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ceftazidime" title="Ceftazidime">ceftazidime</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Oxley_Developments&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Oxley Developments (page does not exist)">Oxley Developments</a> (electronics) are at Ulverston near <a href="/wiki/Conishead_Priory" title="Conishead Priory">Conishead Priory</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Lists_of_schools_in_England#North_West_of_England" title="Lists of schools in England">Lists of schools in England \xc2\xa7&#160;North West of England</a></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Secondary_education">Secondary education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Secondary education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Secondary schools are mostly comprehensive, but Trafford retains a wholly selective school system, and there are some other <a href="/wiki/Grammar_school" title="Grammar school">grammar schools</a> in Lancashire, Wirral, Liverpool and Cumbria.\n</p><p>There are around 345,000 at secondary school in the region, the third highest in England, after <a href="/wiki/South_East_England" title="South East England">South East England</a> and <a href="/wiki/Greater_London" title="Greater London">Greater London</a>. This is around three times as much as there are in <a href="/wiki/North_East_England" title="North East England">North East England</a>. For school <a href="/wiki/Truancy" title="Truancy">truancy</a> the most number of persistent truants are in Manchester with a rate of 7.3%, followed by <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Borough_of_Knowsley" title="Metropolitan Borough of Knowsley">Knowsley</a> with 6.9%, and <a href="/wiki/Blackpool" title="Blackpool">Blackpool</a> with 6.6%. The lowest truancy rate is in <a href="/wiki/South_Ribble" title="South Ribble">South Ribble</a> with 2.4% followed by <a href="/wiki/Ribble_Valley" title="Ribble Valley">Ribble Valley</a> with 2.9% (both in Lancashire).\n</p><p>At A level in 2010, Trafford performed the best and, again like its results at GCSE, is one of the best areas in England. The lowest performing area is, again, Knowsley but followed by Rochdale. Knowsley has had some dreadful results at A-level; <a href="/wiki/Halewood_Academy" title="Halewood Academy">Halewood Academy</a>, its last school sixth-form, closed in 2016; there is now no school-based A-level provision in Knowsley, it is provided by the <a href="/wiki/Knowsley_Community_College" title="Knowsley Community College">Knowsley Community College</a>. For traditional counties, Lancashire gets excellent results at A-level, being one of the best in England. Areas also performing above the England average, in order of results, are Blackpool, Warrington, Wigan, Cheshire West and Chester, Bury, Cumbria, Wirral, and Stockport. Blackpool performs not particularly well at GCSE, yet produces much better results at A level\xe2\x80\x94even better than <a href="/wiki/Cheshire_West_and_Chester" title="Cheshire West and Chester">Cheshire West and Chester</a>, and the third-best in the region.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a Four of these areas are or were part of Cheshire.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. There are forty three FE colleges. The regional LSC was in central Manchester; this is now the SFA and the YPLA.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Universities">Universities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Universities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a Rack</a></i></div></div></div>\n<p>The universities in the North West are listed below:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Manchester" title="University of Manchester">University of Manchester</a>, Manchester \xe2\x80\x93 The <a href="/wiki/List_of_universities_in_the_United_Kingdom_by_enrolment" title="List of universities in the United Kingdom by enrolment">largest single-site university in the UK</a> with 36,907 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Manchester_Metropolitan_University" title="Manchester Metropolitan University">Manchester Metropolitan University</a>, Manchester \xe2\x80\x93 Also one of the country\'s largest universities with 40,420 students \xe2\x80\x93 second-largest university in the region</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Central_Lancashire" title="University of Central Lancashire">UCLAN</a>, Preston \xe2\x80\x93 The University of Central Lancashire in Preston, 28,850 students \xe2\x80\x93 third-largest university in the region</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Liverpool_John_Moores_University" title="Liverpool John Moores University">Liverpool John Moores University</a>, Liverpool \xe2\x80\x93 24,085 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Liverpool" title="University of Liverpool">University of Liverpool</a>, Liverpool \xe2\x80\x93 20,765 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Salford" title="University of Salford">University of Salford</a>, Salford \xe2\x80\x93 20,185 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Lancaster_University" title="Lancaster University">Lancaster University</a>, Lancaster \xe2\x80\x93 17,415 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/The_University_of_Law" class="mw-redirect" title="The University of Law">The University of Law</a>, Chester, Manchester</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Edge_Hill_University" title="Edge Hill University">Edge Hill University</a>, Ormskirk \xe2\x80\x93 15,645 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Chester" title="University of Chester">University of Chester</a>, Chester and Warrington \xe2\x80\x93 15,095 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Bolton" title="University of Bolton">University of Bolton</a>, Bolton \xe2\x80\x93 8,540 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Hope_University" title="Liverpool Hope University">Liverpool Hope University</a>, Liverpool \xe2\x80\x93 8,205 students</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Cumbria" title="University of Cumbria">University of Cumbria</a> \xe2\x80\x93 The region\'s newest university located across Cumbria, parts of Lancashire and London, and formerly known as the Cumbria Institute of the Arts</li></ul>\n<p>Over 60% of university students in the region are native to the region. The region with the next-highest number of students in the North-West is <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire_and_the_Humber" title="Yorkshire and the Humber">Yorkshire and the Humber</a>, so approximately 80% of university students in the area are from the north of England. The region\'s students have the highest proportion of students from so-called low-participation neighbourhoods.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Local_media">Local media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Granada_TV.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>ITV Granada former studios in Castlefield, Manchester</div></div></div>\n<dl><dt>TV</dt></dl>\n<ul><li>Regional news programmes for the Isle of Man, North West England and south of Cumbria \xe2\x80\x93 <i><a href="/wiki/BBC_North_West_Tonight" title="BBC North West Tonight">North West Tonight</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/BBC_North_West" title="BBC North West">BBC North West</a>) and <i><a href="/wiki/Granada_Reports" title="Granada Reports">Granada Reports</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/ITV_Granada" title="ITV Granada">ITV Granada</a>), both based in <a href="/wiki/Salford_Quays" title="Salford Quays">Salford Quays</a> since Autumn 2011 and Spring 2013 respectively.</li>\n<li>Regional news programmes for the north of Cumbria \xe2\x80\x93 <i><a href="/wiki/BBC_Look_North_(North_East_and_Cumbria)" title="BBC Look North (North East and Cumbria)">Look North</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/BBC_North_East_and_Cumbria" title="BBC North East and Cumbria">BBC North East and Cumbria</a>) based in <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_upon_Tyne" title="Newcastle upon Tyne">Newcastle</a> and <i><a href="/wiki/Lookaround" title="Lookaround">Lookaround</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/ITV_Tyne_Tees_%26_Border" title="ITV Tyne Tees &amp; Border">ITV Tyne Tees &amp; Border</a>) based in <a href="/wiki/Gateshead" title="Gateshead">Gateshead</a>.</li>\n<li>Regional news programmes for the <a href="/wiki/West_Craven" title="West Craven">West Craven</a> area of Lancashire, historically in the <a href="/wiki/West_Riding_of_Yorkshire" title="West Riding of Yorkshire">West Riding of Yorkshire</a> \xe2\x80\x93 <i><a href="/wiki/BBC_Look_North_(Yorkshire_and_North_Midlands)" title="BBC Look North (Yorkshire and North Midlands)">Look North</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/ITV_News_Calendar" class="mw-redirect" title="ITV News Calendar">ITV News Calendar</a></i> both based in <a href="/wiki/Leeds" title="Leeds">Leeds</a>. Both are broadcast from the <a href="/wiki/Skipton" title="Skipton">Skipton</a> transmitter which is part of the <a href="/wiki/Emley_Moor" class="mw-redirect" title="Emley Moor">Emley Moor</a> transmitter group.\n<ul><li>N.B. Digital TV comes from <a href="/wiki/Winter_Hill_transmitting_station" title="Winter Hill transmitting station">Winter Hill</a> for the south of the region, and <a href="/wiki/Caldbeck_transmitting_station" title="Caldbeck transmitting station">Caldbeck</a> for Cumbria. <a href="/wiki/Digital_switchover_dates_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Digital switchover dates in the United Kingdom">Digital switchover</a> took place in mid-2009 for Cumbria and late-2009 for the south of the region.</li></ul></li></ul>\n<dl><dt>Radio</dt></dl>\n<ul><li>BBC Radios <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Manchester" title="BBC Radio Manchester">Manchester</a>, <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Merseyside" title="BBC Radio Merseyside">Merseyside</a>, <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Lancashire" title="BBC Radio Lancashire">Lancashire</a> and <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Cumbria" title="BBC Radio Cumbria">Cumbria</a>. National radio comes from <a href="/wiki/Holme_Moss" title="Holme Moss">Holme Moss</a> (for Merseyside, Greater Manchester, and Cheshire) and <a href="/wiki/Sandale_transmitting_station" title="Sandale transmitting station">Sandale</a> for Cumbria. There is a main MW transmitter for the region (and England), over the border in <a href="/wiki/Kirklees" title="Kirklees">Kirklees</a>, at <a href="/wiki/Moorside_Edge_transmitting_station" title="Moorside Edge transmitting station">Moorside Edge</a>.</li>\n<li>Several commercial radio stations including: <a href="/wiki/Real_Radio_North_West" class="mw-redirect" title="Real Radio North class="mw-redirect" title="A576 road">A576</a> roundabout which prints the <i>Guardian</i> (it is owned 50% with the Telegraph and 50% by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Guardian_Print_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Guardian Print Centre (page does not exist)">Guardian Print Centre</a>); it printed the <i>Telegraph</i> until 2008, and is known also as GPC Manchester. From 2008, the <i>Telegraph</i> has been printed at the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Newsprinters&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Newsprinters (page does not exist)">Newsprinters</a> huge site at Knowsley. Newsprinters have a site near Dairy Crest at Knowsley, and prints the <i>Times</i>, <i>Telegraph</i> and <i>Sun</i> titles, near the B5202.\n</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Broughton_Printers&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Broughton Printers (page does not exist)">Broughton Printers</a>, owned by Northern &amp; Shell, print the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Express" title="Daily Express">Express</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Star_(British_newspaper)" class="mw-redirect" title="Daily Star (British newspaper)">Star</a></i> at <a href="/wiki/Fulwood,_Lancashire" title="Fulwood, Lancashire">Fulwood</a> on the B6241 south of the M55/M6 junction, on the same site as the <i>Lancashire Evening Post</i>.\n</p>\n<dl><dt>Magazines</dt></dl>\n<p>Prinovis in Liverpool (Speke) prints <i><a href="/wiki/OK!" title="OK!">OK!</a></i>, the <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sun_(United_Kingdom)" title="The Sun (United Kingdom)">Sun on Sunday</a></i> magazine (<i>Fabulous</i>), and the <i>Sunday Times</i> <a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Times_Magazine" title="The Sunday Times class="mw-redirect" title="St Bris le Vineux">St Bris le Vineux</a>, France\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sport">Sport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Sport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The modern <a href="/wiki/Darts" title="Darts">dart board</a> was invented in 1896 by Lancashire carpenter <a href="/w/index.php?title=Brian_Gamlin&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Brian Gamlin (page does not exist)">Brian Gamlin</a> from Bury, aged 44. <a href="/wiki/Oulton_Park" title="Oulton Park">Oulton Park</a>, in central Cheshire, is the home of the <a href="/wiki/British_Touring_Car_Championship" title="British Touring Car Championship">British Touring Car Championship</a> in June. The <a href="/wiki/International_Netball_Federation" title="International Netball Federation">International Netball Federation</a> is situated in Manchester, home to the <a href="/wiki/National_Squash_Centre" title="National Squash Centre">National Squash Centre</a> and the <a href="/wiki/National_Cycling_Centre" title="National Cycling Centre">National Cycling Centre</a> (<a href="/wiki/Manchester_Velodrome" title="Manchester Velodrome">Manchester Velodrome</a> and <a href="/wiki/British_Cycling" title="British Cycling">British Cycling</a>) at <a href="/wiki/Sportcity" title="Sportcity">Sportcity</a>. The first greyhound racing in the UK was in July 1926 in Manchester at the purpose-built oval <a href="/wiki/Belle_Vue_Stadium" title="Belle Vue Stadium">Belle Vue Stadium</a>. The <a href="/wiki/National_Football_Museum" title="National Football Museum">National Football Museum</a> is in Manchester.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Football">Football</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Football">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Here is a list of the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> and <a href="/wiki/Football_League" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League">Football League</a> teams in the North West. Teams from the north-west have won more than half of all Football League (before 1992) and Premier League seasons with Manchester United having won more than any other team.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Golf">Golf</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" for rugby league teams in the north-west is the <a href="/wiki/Challenge_Cup" title="Challenge Cup">Challenge Cup</a>.\n</p><p>Super League and National League teams in the North West ranked on their <b>(6th)</b></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swimming">Swimming</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Swimming">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/British_Swimming" class="mw-redirect" title="British Swimming">British Swimming</a> have one of its three Intensive Training Centres at the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Central_Stockport" title="Grand Central Stockport">Grand Central Pools</a> in Stockport.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Weather">Weather</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=North_West_England&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Weather">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The North West is generally regarded as having the most average weather in the UK. Temperatures are generally close to the national average. Cumbria usually experiences the most severe weather, with high precipitation in the mountainous regions of the Lake District and Pennines. In winter, the most severe weather occurs in the more exposed and elevated areas of the North West, once again this is mainly the <a href="/wiki/Lake_District" title="Lake District">Lake District</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pennines" title="Pennines">Pennine</a> areas. \nParts of the North West experienced a <a href="/wiki/White_Christmas_(weather)" title="White Christmas (weather)">White Christmas</a> in 2009, and again in 2010, where sleet and snow fell on 25 December.\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/A635" class="mw-redirect" title="A635">A635</a> was closed for almost a month in January 2010 due to high amounts of snowfall.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a During the first quarter of the eighteenth century [after the Treaty of Union], Catholic bishops were banned and priests required to register. Catholics lost their right to vote, hold office, own a gun or a horse worth more than 5 pounds, or live in towns without paying special fees...
